79.2. Ðu þe recysð irahel beheald þu gelædyst swa swa sciep þu sityst ofyr cherubin ætyw <foreign>Qvi regis israhel intende qui deducis uelut ouem ioseph qui sedis super cherubin appare</foreign>.
79.3. Beforan effrem beniamin & manasse awece mihte þine & cume þæt hæle gedo us <foreign>coram effrem beniamin et manasse excita potentiam tuam et ueni ut saluos facias nos</foreign>.
79.4. Drihtyn god mægyna gecyrr us & ætyw ansyne þine & hale we beoð <foreign>Domine deus uirtutum conuerte nos et ostende faciem tuam et salui erimus</foreign>.
79.5. Drihtyn god mægyna hu lange yrsast þu on gebede þeowys þinys <foreign>Domine deus uirtutum quousque irasceris in orationem serui tui</foreign>.
79.6. Þu fedyst us hlafe teara & scenc sylyst us on tearum on gemete <foreign>cybabis nos pane lacrimarum et potum dabis nobis in lacrimis in mensura</foreign>.
79.7. Ðu gesettyst us in wiðcwedennysse neahgeburum urum & fynd ure bysmrydon us <foreign>Posuisti nos in contradictionem uicinis nostris et inimici nostri deriserunt nos</foreign>.
79.8. Drihtyn god mægyna gecyrr us & ætyw ansyne þine & hale we beoð <foreign>Domine deus uirtutum conuerte nos et ostende faciem tuam et salui erimus</foreign>.
79.9. Wingeard of egyptum þu afyrdyst þu awvrpe þeoda & plantodyst hi <foreign>Uineam ex egypto transtulisti eiecisti gentes et plantasti eam</foreign>.
79.10. Weg þu dydyst on gesihðe his & þu plantodyst wyrtruman hys & gefyllyd ys eorðe <foreign>Viam fecisti in conspectu eius et plantasti radices eius et repleta est terra</foreign>.
79.11. Ofyrwreah muntas sceadu his & treow his cedyrbiem godys <foreign>Operuit montes umbra eius et arbusta eius cedros dei</foreign>.
79.12. Þu aþenydyst palmtwigu his oð to sæ & oð þæt flod setyne hys <foreign>Extendisti palmites eius usque ad mare et usque ad flumen propagines eius</foreign>.
79.13. Tohwon asettyst þu stanweall his & winrypað hi ealle þa þa leorað weg <foreign>Vtquid deposuisti maceriam eius et uindemiant eam omnes qui transeunt uiam</foreign>.
79.14. Gebrytte vel geblæcte þa efyr wuda & syndrig wildeor hyðynde wæs hi <foreign>Exterminauit eam aper de silua et singularis ferus depastus est eam</foreign>.
79.15. Drihtyn god mægyna gecyrr nu geloca of hefyne & geseoh & geneosa wingeard þisne <foreign>Domine deus uirtutum conuerte nunc respice de celo et uide et uisita uineam istam</foreign>.
79.16. & gerece hine þone geplantode swiðre þin & ofyr sunu mannys þone þu getrymydyst þe <foreign>et dirige eam quam plantauit dextera tua et super filium hominis quem confirmasti tibi</foreign>.
79.17. Onælyd mid fyre & agotyn of handa fram þreaunge andwlitan þinys forwurðað <foreign>Incensa igni et effossa manu ab increpatione uultus tui peribunt</foreign>.
79.18. Sy hand þin ofyr were swiðre þinre & ofyr sunu mannys þone þu getrymydyst þe <foreign>Fiat manus tua super uirum dextere tue et super filium hominis quem confirmasti tibi</foreign>.
79.19. & we ne gewitað fram þe ðu geliffæstast us & nama þin we gecigeað <foreign>et non discedimus a te uiuificabis nos et nomen tuum inuocabimus</foreign>.
79.20. Drihtyn god mægna gecyrr us & ætyw ansyne þine & hale we beoð <foreign>Domine deus uirtutum conuerte nos et ostende faciem tuam et salui erimus</foreign>.
80.2. Wunsumiað gode fultume urum wynsumiað gode iacobys <foreign>Exvltate deo adiutori nostro iubilate deo iacob</foreign>.
80.3. Nymað sealm & syllað tympanan hearpan wynsume mid citran <foreign>Sumite psalmum et date tympanum psalterium iocundum cum cythara</foreign>.
80.4. Singað on fruman monðys byman on dæge on mærum symbylnysse eowre <foreign>Canite in initio mensis tuba in die insignis sollempnitatis uestre</foreign>.
80.5. Forþon bebod on israhel ys & dom gode iacobys <foreign>Quia preceptum in israhel est et iudicium deo iacob</foreign>.
80.6. Cyðnysse on ioseph sette hine þonne he uteode of eorðan aegypta tungan þa he ne gecnew he gehyrde <foreign>testimonium in ioseph posuit eum dum exiret de terra aegypti linguam quam non nouerat audiuit</foreign>.
80.7. He acyrde fram byrnyndum hricg his hand his on binne þeowudon <foreign>diuertit ab oneribus dorsum eius manus eius in cophino seruierunt</foreign>.
80.8. On geswince þu gecygdyst me & ic gefreode þe & ic gehyrde þe on digylnysse stormys ic fandvde þin to wætra wiðcwedynnysse <foreign>In tribulatione inuocasti me et liberaui te exaudiui te in abscondito tempestatis probaui te ad aquas contradictionis</foreign>.
80.9. Gehyr folc min & ic sprece to israhel & ic cyðe þe gif þu me gehyryst <foreign>Audi populus meus et loquar israhel et testificabor tibi israhel si me audieris</foreign>.
80.10. Ne bið on þe god niwe ne þu wurðast god fremdne <foreign>non erit in te deus recens neque adorabis deum alienum</foreign>.
80.11. Ic soðlice eom drihtyn god þin þe gelædde þe of lande aegypta tobræd muð þinne & ic gefylle þone <foreign>Ego enim sum dominus deus tuus qui eduxi te de terra egypti dilato os tuum et ego adimplebo illud</foreign>.
80.12. & ne gehyrde folc min stefne mine & israhel ne behealdyð me <foreign>et non audiuit populus meus uocem meam et israhel non intendit mihi</foreign>.
80.13. & ic forlet hi æftyr lustum heortan hyra & hi gað on lustum hyra <foreign>Et dimisi eos secundum desideria cordis eorum et ibunt in uoluntatibus suis</foreign>.
80.14. Gef folc min gehyrde me israhel gif hit o wegas mine eode <foreign>Se pleps mea audisset me israhel si in uiis meis ambulasset</foreign>.
80.15. To nohte feond hyra ic geeaðmodode & ofyr þa geswencyndan hi ic onsende hand mine <foreign>ad nihilum inimicos eorum humiliassem et super tribulantes eos immisissem manum meam</foreign>.
80.16. Fynd drihtnys leogynde syndon vel wæron him & bið tid hyra on ecnysse <foreign>Inimici domini mentiti sunt ei et erit tempus eorum in eternum</foreign>.
80.17. Fedde hi of smeruwe hwætys & of stane mid hunige he gereordode hi <foreign>Cibauit eos ex adipe frumenti et de petra melle saturauit eos</foreign>.
81.1. God stod on gesomnunge goda on midle soðlice god tosceadyð <foreign>Devs stetit in sinagoga deorum in medio autem deus discernit</foreign>.
81.2. Hu lange demað ge unrihtwisnysse vel onsyne synfulra ge nymað <foreign>Quousque iudicatis iniquitatem et facies peccantium sumitis</foreign>.
81.3. Demað fædyrleasne vel wedlan heanne & þearfan gerihtwisiað <foreign>Iudicate pupillo et egeno humilem et pauperem iustificate</foreign>.
81.4. Genergeað þearfan & wædlan of hand synfulra gefreogeað <foreign>Eripite pauperem et egenum de manu peccatorum liberate</foreign>.
81.5. Nyston ne ne ongeton on þystrum gað beoð onstyryde ealle staþolas eorðan <foreign>Nescierunt neque intellexerunt in tenebris ambulant nouebuntur omnia fundamenta terre</foreign>.
81.6. Ic cwæð godas ge syndon & bearn þæs hean ealle <foreign>Ego dixi dii estis et filii excelsi omnes</foreign>.
81.7. Ge soðlice swa swa menn sweltað & swa swa an of ealdormannum ge feallað <foreign>Vos autem sicut homines moriemini et sicut unus de principibus cadetis</foreign>.
81.8. Aris god dem eorðan forþam þu yrfeweardast on eallum þeodum <foreign>Exurge deus iudica terram quoniam tu hereditabis in omnibus gentibus</foreign>.
82.2. God hwylc gelice bið þe ne swiga þu ne ne bewere god <foreign>Devs qvis similis erit tibi ne taceas neque conpescaris deus</foreign>.
82.3. Forþan efneþa fynd þine hleoðrodon & þa þe þe feodon ahofon upp heafud <foreign>Quoniam ecce inimici tui sonauerunt et qui te oderunt extulerunt caput</foreign>.
82.4. On folc þin gefædlice þohton geþeaht & þohton ongen halgum þinum <foreign>In plebem tuam astute cogitauerunt consilium et cogitauerunt aduersus sanctos tuos</foreign>.
82.5. Cwædon cumað tostregdyn we hi of þeode & ne bið gemyngod nama ma <foreign>Dixerunt uenite disperdamus eos ex gente et non memorabitur nomen israhel amplius</foreign>.
82.6. Forþan þohton geþafunge on an ongen þe cyðnysse gestihtodon <foreign>Quoniam cogitauerunt consensum in unum aduersum te testamentum disposuerunt</foreign>.
82.7. Geteld idumea hyra & ismahela moab & agar <foreign>Tabernacula idumeorum et ismahelitum moab et agareni</foreign>.
82.8. Gebal & ammon & amalech & fremde mid eardiyndum tir mægðe <foreign>gebal et amon et amalech et aligenigene cum habitantibus tirum</foreign>.
82.9. & soðlice assur samod cymð mid him gewordyne synd on fengnysse bearnum loth <foreign>Etenim assur simul uenit cum illis facti sunt in susceptionem filiis loth</foreign>.
82.10. Doa him swa swa madian & sisarra swa swa iabin on burnan cison <foreign>Fac illis sicut madian et sisare sicut iabin in torrente cison</foreign>.
82.11. Forwurdon on endor gewordyne synd swa swa sciern eorðan <foreign>disperierunt in endor facti sunt sicut stercus terre</foreign>.
82.12. Sete ealdormenn hyra swa swa oreb & zeb & zebee & salmana ealle ealdormenn hyra <foreign>Pone principes eorum sicut horeb zeb et zebee et salmana omnes principes eorum</foreign>.
82.13. Þa cwædon yrfeweardnysse gesettyn we us haligportic godys <foreign>qui dixerunt hereditate possideamus nobis sanctuarium dei</foreign>.
82.14. God min sete hi swa swa hweowul & swa swa hielm beforan ansyne windys & <foreign>Deus meus pone illos ut rotam et sicut stipulam ante faciem uenti et</foreign>.
82.15. Swa fyr þæt forbærnyð wudas swa swa lig forbærne muntas <foreign>sicut ignis qui conburit siluas uelut si flamma incendat montes</foreign>.
82.16. Swa þu iehtyst hi on storme þinum & on yrre þinum gedrefyst hi <foreign>Ita persequeris eos in tempestate tua et in ira tua conturbabis eos</foreign>.
82.17. Gefyll ansyne hyra mid orwurðe & seceaþ naman þinne drihtyn <foreign>Imple facies eorum ignominia et querant nomen tuum domine</foreign>.
82.18. Syn gescynde & gedrefde on woruld worulde & onscuniyn & forwurðyn <foreign>Confundantur et conturbentur in seculum seculi et reuereantur et pereant</foreign>.
82.19. & oncnæwyn forðon nama þe drihtyn þu ana se heahsta ofyr ealle eorðan <foreign>et cognoscant quia nomen tibi dominus tu solus altisimus super omnem terram</foreign>.
83.2. Hu lufiyndlic synd geteld þin drihtyn mægna <foreign>Qvam amabilia sunt tabernacula tua domine uirtutum</foreign>.
83.3. Gewilnode & asprang sawl min on cafyrtune drihtnys heorte min & flæsc min upahofon on god lyfigyndne <foreign>Concupiuit et defecit anima mea in atria domini cor meum et caro mea exultauerunt in deum uiuum</foreign>.
83.4. & soðlice spearwa gemetyð him hus & turtle nest hwær gesetyð briddas his wibed þin drihtyn mægyna cyning min & god min <foreign>etenim passer inuenit sibi domum et turtur nidum ubi reponat pullos suos altaria tua domine uirtutum rex meus et deus meus</foreign>.
83.5. Eadige þa þe eardiað on huse þinum drihtyn on woruld worulde hergeað þe <foreign>Beati qui habitant in domo tua domine in seculum seculi laudabunt te</foreign>.
83.6. Eadig wer þæs ys fultum from þe drihtyn upstige on heortan his gestihtode <foreign>Beatus uir cuius est auxilium abs te domine ascensus in corde eius disposuit</foreign>.
83.7. On dene tearyna on stowe þa þu gestihtodyst him <foreign>in conualle lacrimarum in locum quem disposuisti eis</foreign>.
83.8. & soðlice bletsunge sylyð se æ sealde gongað of mægyne on mægyn bið gesewyn god goda on syon <foreign>Etenim benedictionem dabit qui legem dedit ambulabunt de uirtute in uirtutem uidebitur deus deorum in sion</foreign>.
83.9. Drihtyn god mægyna gehyr bene mine mid earum onfoh god iacobys <foreign>Domine deus uirtutum exaudi precem meam auribus percipe deus iacob</foreign>.
83.10. Gescyldynd ure geloca god & geseoh on ansyne cristes þinys <foreign>Protector noster aspice deus et respice in faciem christi tui</foreign>.
83.11. Forþon betre ys dæg on an on cafertunum þinum ofyr þusynd ic geceas aworpyn beon on huse godys ma þonne eardian on geteldum synnfulra <foreign>Quia melior est dies una in atris tuis super milia elegi abiectus esse in domo dei magis quam habitare in tabernaculis peccatorum</foreign>.
83.12. Forðan mildheortnysse & soðfæstnysse lufude drihtyn gyfe & wuldur sylyð god : <foreign>Quoniam misericordiam et ueritatem diligit dominus gratiam et gloriam dabit deus</foreign>.
83.13. Drihtyn ne bescyryð godum gongynde on unsceðfulnysse drihtyn god mægyna eadig mann se þe gehihtyd on þe <foreign>Dominus non priuabit bonis ambulantes in innocentia domine deus uirtutum beatus homo qui sperat in te</foreign>.
84.2. Þu bletsodyst drihtyn eorðan þine þu acyrdyst hæftnyd Iacobys <foreign>Benedixisti domine terram tuam auertisti captiuitatem iacob</foreign>.
84.3. Ðu geedleanodyst unrihtwisnysse folcys þinys þu ofyrwruge ealle synna heora <foreign>Remisisti iniquitatem plebis tue operuisti omnia peccata eorum</foreign>.
84.4. Þu gestildyst eall yrre þin þu acyrdyst fram yrre æbyligþe þinre <foreign>Mitigasti omnem iram tuam auertisti ab ira indignationis tue</foreign>.
84.5. Gecyrr us god halwenda ure & acyrr yrre þin fram us <foreign>Conuerte nos deus salutaris noster et auerte iram tuam a nobis</foreign>.
84.6. Þæt na on ecnysse yrsige us ne ne aþene þu yrre þin fram cynne on cynn <foreign>ut non in eternum irascaris nobis neque extendas iram tuam a progenie in progeniem</foreign>.
84.7. God þu forcyrrynde þu geliffæstast us & folc þin bið geblissod on þe <foreign>deus tu conuertens uiuificabis nos et plebs tua letabitur in te</foreign>.
84.8. Ætyw us drihtyn mildheortnysse þine & hæle þine syle us <foreign>Ostende nobis domine misericordiam tuam et salutare tuum da nobis</foreign>.
84.9. Ic gehyre hwæt sprece on me drihtyn god forþan sprecð sybbe on folce his & ofyr haligan his & on hi þe beoð gecyrryde to him <foreign>Audiam quid loquatur in me dominus deus quoniam loquetur pacem in plebem suam et super sanctos suos et in eos qui conuertuntur ad ipsum</foreign>.
84.10. Þeahhwæðere nieh ondrædynde hyne hæle his þæt oneardige wuldur on eorðan ure <foreign>Verumtamen prope timentibus eum salutare ipsius ut inhabitet gloria in terra nostra</foreign>.
84.11. Mildheortnys & soðfæstnys tosomnebecomon him rihtwisnys & sybb clyppynde wæron hi <foreign>Misericordia et ueritas obuiauerunt sibi iustitia et pax conplexe sunt se</foreign>.
84.12. Soðfæstnys of eorðan upcumyn ys & rihtwisnyss of heofone forðlocode <foreign>Ueritas de terra orta est et iustitia de celo prospexit</foreign>.
84.13. & soðlice drihtyn sylyð fremsumnysse & eorðe ure sylyð wæstm his <foreign>Etenim dominus dabit benignitatem et terra nostra dabit fructum suum</foreign>.
84.14. Rihtwisnys beforan him gongyð & gesetyð on wege gongas his <foreign>Justitia ante eum ambulabit et ponet in uia gressus suos</foreign>.
85.1. Onhyld drihtyn eare þin to me & gehyr me forþan wædla & þearfa eom ic <foreign>Inclina domine aurem tuam ad me et exaudi me quoniam egenus et pauper sum ego</foreign>.
85.2. Geheald sawle mine forðon halig ic eom halne gedo þeow þinne god min gehihtynde on þe <foreign>Custodi animam meam quoniam sanctus sum saluum fac seruum tuum deus meus sperantem in te</foreign>.
85.3. Gemyltsa me drihtyn forðon to þe ic clypige ealne dæg <foreign>Miserere mihi domine quoniam ad te clamaui tota die</foreign>.
85.4. Geblissa sawle þeowys þinys forþon to þe drihtyn ic hof sawl mine <foreign>letifica animam serui tui qui ad te domine leuaui animam meam</foreign>.
85.5. Forþon þu drihtyn wynsum & milde eart & genihtsum on mildheortnysse eallum gecigyndum þe <foreign>Quoniam tu domine suauis ac mitis es et copiosus in misericordia omnibus inuocantibus te</foreign>.
85.6. Mid earum onfoh drihtyn gebed min & beheald stefne bene minre <foreign>Auribus percipe domine orationem meam et intende uoci deprecationis mee</foreign>.
85.7. On dæge geswincys minys ic clypige to þe forþon þu gehyrdyst me <foreign>In die tribulationis mee clamaui ad te quoniam exaudisti me</foreign>.
85.8. Nys gelice þe on godum drihtyn & nys æftyr worc þin <foreign>Non est similis tibi in diis domine et non est secundum opera tua</foreign>.
85.9. Ealle þeoda swa hwylce þu dydyst cumað & wurðiað beforan þe drihtyn & wurðiað naman þinne <foreign>Omnes gentes quascumque fecisti uenient et adhorabunt coram te domine et honorificabunt nomen tuum</foreign>.
85.10. Forþon micyl eart þu & doynde wundru þu eart god ana <foreign>Quoniam magnus es tu et faciens mirabilia tu est deus solus</foreign>.
85.11. Gelæd me drihtyn on wege þinum & ic gange on soðfæstnysse þinre blissige heorte min þæt heo ondræde naman þinne <foreign>Deduc me domine in uia tua et ambulabo in ueritate tua letetur cor meum ut timeat nomen tuum</foreign>.
85.12. Ic andytte þe drihtyn god min on eallre heortan minre & ic arie naman þinne on ecnysse <foreign>confitebor tibi domine deus meus in toto corde meo et honorificabo nomen tuum in eternum</foreign>.
85.13. Forðon mildheortnys þin micyl ys ofyr me & þu generedyst sawle mine of helle þære nyðyrran <foreign>Quoniam misericordia tua magna est super me et eripuisti animam meam ex inferno inferiore</foreign>.
85.14. God þa unrihtwis arison on me & gesomnung mihtigra sohton sawle mine & ne foresetton þe beforan gesihðe his <foreign>Deus iniusti insurrexerunt in me et sinagoga potentium quesierunt animam meam et non proposuerunt te ante conspectum suum</foreign>.
85.15. & þu drihtyn god min mildsiynd & mildheort geþyldig & swiðe mildheort & soðfæst <foreign>Et tu domine deus meus miserator et misericors patiens et multum misericors et uerax</foreign>.
85.16. Geloca on me & milsa min syle mihte cnafan þinum & halne doa sunu þeowyne þinre <foreign>Respice in me et miserere mei da potestatem puero tuo et saluum fac filium ancille tue</foreign>.
85.17. Doa mid me drihtyn tacn on gode þæt hi geseon þa þe me feodun & syn gescynde forðan þu drihtyn þu gefultumdyst me & frefriynd eart þu me <foreign>Fac mecum domine signum in bono ut uideant qui me oderunt et confundantur quoniam tu domine adiuuasti me et consolatus es me</foreign>.
86.1. Staðolas his on muntum halygum <foreign>Fvndamenta eivs in montibus sanctis</foreign>.
86.2. Lufað drihtyn gatu sionys ofyr ealle geteld iacobys <foreign>diligit dominus portas sion super omnia tabernacula iacob</foreign>.
86.3. Wuldorfæste gecwedyne synd be þe ciestre godys <foreign>Gloriosa dicta sunt de te ciuitas dei</foreign>.
86.4. Gemyndig raabys & babilonys wityndum þe efneþa fremede & tyrus & folc & sigylhearwyna þas wærun on þære <foreign>memor ero raab et babilonis scientibus te ecce aligenigene et tyrus et populus ethiopum hi fuerunt in ea</foreign>.
86.5. Modor sionys cwyð mann & mann gewordyn ys on þære & he gestaðolode hi se hiehsta <foreign>Mater sion dicet homo homo factus est in ea et ipse fundauit eam altissimus</foreign>.
86.6. Drihtyn sægyð on gewritum folca his & ealdormonna hyra þa wæron on þære <foreign>Dominus narrabit in scripturis populorum suorum et principum eorum qui fuerunt in ea</foreign>.
86.7. Swa swa blissiyndra eallra ure eardungstow is on þe <foreign>Sicut letantium omnium nostrum habitatio est in te</foreign>.
87.2. Drihtyn god hæle minre on dæge ic clypige & on nihte beforan þe <foreign>Domine devs salutis mee in die clammaui et nocte coram te</foreign>.
87.3. Ingæð gebed min on gesihðe þinre onhyld eare þin to bene minre drihtyn <foreign>Intret oratio mea in conspectu tuo inclina aurem tuam ad precem meam domine</foreign>.
87.4. Forðan gefyllyd ys mid yflum sawl min & lif min on helle togenealæcyð <foreign>Quia repleta est malis anima mea et uita mea in infernvm adpropiauit</foreign>.
87.5. Geteald ic eom mid þam adunstigyndum on seað gewordyn ic eom swa swa mann butan fultume <foreign>Estimatus sum cum descendentibus in lacum factus sum sicut homo sine adiutorio</foreign>.
87.6. Betux deade freoh swa swa gewundode slæpynde aworpyne on byrgynnum þara þu ne gemundyst ma & cuðlice hi of handa þinre adrifyne synd <foreign>inter mortuos liber sicut uulnerati dormientes proiecti in monumentis quorum non meministi amplius et quidem ipsi de manu tua expulsi sunt</foreign>.
87.7. Hi gesettun me on seaðe þan nyðyrran on þystrum & on sceade deaðys <foreign>Posuerunt me in lacum inferiorem in tenebris et in umbra mortis</foreign>.
87.8. On me getrymyd ys yrre þin & ealle upahafynnyssa mine ofyr me inngelæddyst <foreign>In me confirmata est ira tua et omnes elationes meas super me induxisti</foreign>.
87.9. Feorr þu dydyst cuðan mine fram me hi gesetton me on onscununge him geseald ic eom & ut ic ne eode <foreign>Longe fecisti notos meos a me posuerunt me in abominationem sibi traditus sum et non egrediebar</foreign>.
87.10. Eagan mine geuntrumude synd for wædlnysse ic clypode to þe drihtne ealne dæg ic aðenyde handa mine to þe <foreign>Oculi mei infirmati sunt pre inopia clamaui ad te domine tota die expandi manus meas ad te</foreign>.
87.11. Ac deadum dest þu wundor oððe læcas aweccað & andyttað þe <foreign>Numquid mortuis facies mirabilia aut medici resuscitabunt et confitebuntur tibi</foreign>.
87.12. Ah sægð ænig on byrgynne mildheortnysse þine & soðfæstnysse þine on forlorynnysse <foreign>Numquid enarrabit aliquis in sepulchro misericordiam tuam et ueritatem tuam in perditionem</foreign>.
87.13. Ac beoð oncnæwyn on þystrum wundru þine oððe rihtwisnysse þine on eorðan ofyrgytulnysse <foreign>Numquid cognoscentur in tenebris mirabilia tua et iustitia tua in terra obliuionis</foreign>.
87.14. & ic to þe drihtyn ic clypige & on morgynne gebed min forcymð þe <foreign>Et ego ad te domine clamaui et mane oratio mea preueniet te</foreign>.
87.15. Tohwon drihtyn onwegadrifyst þu gebed min acyrryst þu ansyne þine fram me <foreign>Vt quid domine repellis orationem meam auertis faciem tuam a me</foreign>.
87.16. Wædla eom ic & on geswincum vel winnum fram iuguðe minre uppahafyn soðlice geeaðmodud ic eom & gescynd <foreign>Egens sum ego et in laboribus a iuuentute mea exaltatus autem humiliatus sum et confusus</foreign>.
87.17. On me þurhferdon yrre þine & brogan þine gedrefdon me <foreign>In me pertransierunt ire tue et terrores tui conturbauerunt me</foreign>.
87.18. Ymbeodon me swa swa wætyr ealne dæg ymbsealdon me samod <foreign>Circumdederunt me sicut aqua tota die circumdederunt me simul</foreign>.
87.19. Ðu afeorrodyst from me freond & þone niehstan & cuðan mine fram yrmðe <foreign>Elongasti a me amicum et proximum et notos meos a miseria</foreign>.
88.2. Mildheortnysse þine drihtyn on ecnysse ic singe on cneorysse & cynne ic forðsæcge soðfæstnysse þine on muðe minum <foreign>Misericordias tuas domine in eternum cantabo in generatione et progenie pronuntiabo ueritatem tuam in ore meo</foreign>.
88.3. Forþon þu cwæde on ecnysse mildheortnyss bið getymbryd on hefynum byð gegearwud soðfæstnyss þin <foreign>Quoniam dixisti in eternum misericordia edificabitur in celis preparabitur ueritas tua</foreign>.
88.4. Ic gestihtode cyðnysse gecorynum minum ic swor dauid þeowe minum <foreign>Disposui testamentum electis meis iuraui dauid seruo meo</foreign>.
88.5. Oð on ecnysse ic gegearwige sæd þin & ic getinbrie on woruld worulde setl þin <foreign>usque in eternum preparabo semen tuum et edificabo in seculum seculi sedem tuam</foreign>.
88.6. Andyttað hefonas wundru þine drihtyn & soðfæstnysse þine on cyricean haligra <foreign>Confitebuntur celi mirabilia tua domine et ueritatem tuam in ecclesia sanctorum</foreign>.
88.7. Forþan hwylc on wolcnum efynlæht drihtne oððe hwylc gelice bið gode betwuh bearn godys <foreign>Quoniam quis in nubibus equabitur domino aut quis similis erit deo inter filios dei</foreign>.
88.8. God se wuldrað on geþæhte haligra mycyl & to ondrædynne ofyr ealle þa þe on ymbhwyrfte his synd <foreign>Deus qui gloficatur in consilio sanctorum magnus et metuendus super omnes qui in circuitu eius sunt</foreign>.
88.9. Drihtyn god mægyna hwylc gelic þe mihtig eart drihtyn & soðfæstnyss þin on ymbhwyrfte þinum <foreign>Domine deus uirtutum quis similis tibi potens es domine et ueritas tua in circuitu tuo</foreign>.
88.10. Þu wealdyst mihte sæs onstyrenysse soðlice yða hys þu mildsast <foreign>Tu dominaris potestatis maris motum autem fluctuum eius tu mitigas</foreign>.
88.11. Þu geeaðmododost swa swa þone gewundydan ofyrmodan & on mægne earmys þinys þu tostenctyst fynd þine <foreign>Tu humiliasti sicut uulneratum superbum et in uirtute brachii tui dispersisti inimicos tuos</foreign>.
88.12. Ðine synd hefonas & þin ys eorðe ymbhwyrft eorðyna & gefyllnysse hys þu gestaðolodyst <foreign>Tui sunt celi et tua est terra orbem terrarum et plenitudinem eius tu fundasti</foreign>.
88.13. Norðdæl & sæ þu gesceope & on naman þinum gefeoð <foreign>Aquilonem et mare tu creasti tabor et hermon in nomine tuo exultabunt</foreign>.
88.14. Þinne earm mid mihte sy getrymyd hand þin & syn uppahafyn seo swiðre þin <foreign>tuum brachium cum potentia firmetur manus tua et exaltetur dextera tua</foreign>.
88.15. Rihtwisnyss & dom gegearwung setlys þinys mildheortnyss & soðfæstnys foregað beforan ansyne þinre <foreign>iustitia et iudicium preparatio sedis tue misericordia et ueritas preibunt ante faciem tuam</foreign>.
88.16. Eadig folc þe wat wynsumnysse drihtyn on leohte andwlitan þinys gaað <foreign>beatus populus qui scit iubilationem domine in lumine uultus tui ambulabunt</foreign>.
88.17. & on naman þinum gefeoð ealne dæg & on þinre rihtwisnysse beoð uppahafyn <foreign>et in nomine tuo exultabunt tota die et in tua iustitia exaltabuntur</foreign>.
88.18. Forþan wuldur mægnys hyra þu eart & on welgelicydum þinum bið upahafyn horn ure <foreign>Quoniam gloria uirtutis eorum tu es et in beneplacito tuo exaltabitur cornu nostrum</foreign>.
88.19. Forþon drihtnys ys getruwung & þæs halgan cyningys ures <foreign>Quoniam domini est adsumptio et sancti israhel regis nostri</foreign>.
88.20. Þa sprecynde þu wære on gesihðe bearnum þinum & þu cwæde ic sette fultum ofyr þone mihtigan & ic uppahof gecoryne of folce minum <foreign>Tunc locutus es in aspectu filiis tuis et dixisti posui adiutorium super potentem et exaltaui electum de plebe mea</foreign>.
88.21. Ic gemette dauid þeowan minne on ele halgum minum ic smyryde hine <foreign>Inueni dauid seruum meum in oleo sancto meo unxi eum</foreign>.
88.22. Hand soðlice min gefultumað him & earm min gestrongað hine <foreign>Manus enim mea auxiliabitur ei et brachium meum confortabit eum</foreign>.
88.23. Nowiht fromað se feond on him & suna unrihtwisnysse ne sceðþyð him <foreign>Nihil proficiet inimicus in eo et filius iniquitatis non nocebit ei</foreign>.
88.24. & ic forceorfe fynd his fram ansyne his & feogynde hine on fleam ic gecyrre <foreign>Et concidam inimicos eius a facie ipsius et odientes eum in fugam conuertam</foreign>.
88.25. & soðfæstnys min & mildheortnys min mid him & on naman minum bið upahafyn horn his <foreign>Et ueritas mea et misericordia mea cum ipso et in nomine meo exaltabitur cornu eius</foreign>.
88.26. & ic gesette on sæ hand his & on flodum swiðran his <foreign>Et ponam in mari manum eius et in fluminibus dexteram eius</foreign>.
88.27. He gecigyð me fædyr min eart þu god min & andfenge hæle minre <foreign>Ipse inuocauit me pater meus es tu deus meus et susceptor salutis meae</foreign>.
88.28. & ic frumcennyde sette hine heane fore cynigum eorðe <foreign>Et ego primogenitum ponam illum excelsum pre regibus terre</foreign>.
88.29. On ecnysse ic gehealde him mildheortnysse mine & cyðnysse min getrywe him <foreign>In eternum seruabo illi misericordiam meam et testamentum meum fidele ipsi</foreign>.
88.30. & ic sette on woruld worulde setl his & þrymsetl his swa swa dægas hefynys <foreign>Et ponam in seculum seculi sedem eius et thronum eius sicut dies celi</foreign>.
88.31. Gef forlætað bearn his æ mine & on domum minum ne gangað <foreign>Si dereliquerint filii eius legem meam et in iudiciis meis non ambulauerint</foreign>.
88.32. Gif gerihtwisunge mine besmitað & bebodu mine ne healdað <foreign>Si iustificationes meas profanauerint et mandata mea non custodierint</foreign>.
88.33. Ic neosie on worde unrihtwisnysse hyra & on swingyllum synna hyra <foreign>Visitabo in uirga iniquitates eorum et in uerberibus peccata eorum</foreign>.
88.34. Mildheortnysse soðlice mine ic ne tostregde fram him ne ic ne sceðþe on soðfæstnysse minre <foreign>Misericordiam autem meam non dispergam ab eo neque nocebo in ueritate mea</foreign>.
88.35. Ne ic ne besmite cyðnysse mine & þa þe forðgað of welerum minum ic ne do to bysmre <foreign>neque profanabo testamentum meum et que procedunt de labiis meis non faciam irrita</foreign>.
88.36. Æne ic swor on halgum minum gef ic ic leoge <foreign>Semel iuraui in sancto meo si dauid mentiar</foreign>.
88.37. Sæd his on ecnysse wunað <foreign>semen eius in eternum manebit</foreign>.
88.38. & setl his swa swa sunna on gesihðe mine & swa swa monæ fullfremed on ecnysse & cyðnysse on hefone getrywe <foreign>et sedes eius sicut sol in conspectu meo et sicut luna perfecta in eternum et testis in celo fidelis</foreign>.
88.39. Þu soðlice onwegadryfe & forhogdyst & ældyst crist þinne <foreign>Tu uero reppulisti et spreuisti distulisti cristum tuum</foreign>.
88.40. Acyrdyst cyðnysse þeowys þinys þu besmite on eorðan halignysse his <foreign>auertisti testamentum serui tui profanasti in terra santitatem eius</foreign>.
88.41. Þu towurpe ealle stanweallas his þu gesettyst trymynysse his on fyrhto <foreign>Destruxisti omnes macerias eius posuisti munitiones eius in formidinem</foreign>.
88.42. Gereafedon hine ealle þa geleornydan on weg gewordyn ys on edwit niehgeburum his <foreign>Diripuerunt eum omnes transeuntes uiam factus est in obprobrium uicinis suis</foreign>.
88.43. Þu upahofe þa swiðran feonda his þu geblissodyst ealle fynd his <foreign>Exaltasti dexteram inimicorum eius letificasti omnes inimicos eius</foreign>.
88.44. Þu acyrdyst fultum swurdys his & ne eart gefultumiynde hi on gefeohte <foreign>Auertisti adiutorium gladii eius et non est auxiliatus ei in bello</foreign>.
88.45. Þu tolysdyst hine from geclæsnunge & setl his on eorðan gecnysydyst <foreign>Dissoluisti eum ab emundatione et sedem eius in terra conlisisti</foreign>.
88.46. Gewonodyst dægys tida his þu þurhtuge hine gedrefydnysse <foreign>Minorasti dies temporum eius perfudisti eum confusione</foreign>.
88.47. Hu lange drihtyn yrsast þu on ende byrnyð swa swa fyr yrre þin <foreign>Usquequo domine irasceris in finem exardescit sicut ignis ira tua</foreign>.
88.48. Gemyne drihtyn hwæt min sped nalys soðlice idyllice þu gesettyst bearn manna <foreign>Memorare domine que mea substantia non enim uane constituisti filios hominum</foreign>.
88.49. Hwylc ys mann se ðe lifge & ne geseah deað oððe hwilc generyd sawl his of hand helle <foreign>Quis est homo qui uiuit et non uidebit mortem aut quis eruet animam suam de manu inferi</foreign>.
88.50. Hwær synd mildheortnysse þine þa ealdan drihtyn swa swa þu swore dauide on soðfæstnysse þinre <foreign>Vbi sunt misericordie tue antique domine sicut iurasti dauid in ueritate tua</foreign>.
88.51. Gemyndig beo þu edwit þeowa þinra þæt ic gesyngalade on scete minum monigra þeoda <foreign>Memor esto obprobrii seruorum tuorum quod continui in sinu meo multarum gentium</foreign>.
88.52. Þæt edwiton fynd þine drihtyn þæt eðwiton onwendydnysse cristys þinys <foreign>Quod exprobrauerunt inimici tui domine quod exprobrauerunt commotationem cristi tui</foreign>.
88.53. Gebletsod drihtyn on ecnysse sy sy <foreign>Benedictus dominus in eternum fiat fiat</foreign>.
89.1. Drihtyn gebeorh eart þu us from cneorysse & cynne <foreign>Domine refvgivm factus es nobis a generatione et progenie</foreign>.
89.2. Ærþon wæron muntas oððe wære getrymyd ymbhwyrft eorðan from woruld & oð on worulde þu eart god <foreign>Priusquam fierent montes aut formaretur orbis terre a seculo et usque in seculum tu es deus</foreign>.
89.3. Ne acyr þu mann on eaðmodnysse & cwæde beoð gecyrryde bearn manna <foreign>Ne auertas hominem in humilitate et dixisti conuertimini filii hominum</foreign>.
89.4. Forþan þusynd geara ær eagan þine swa swa dæg gyrstan se forðgewat swa swa hyrde on niht <foreign>Quoniam mille anni ante oculos tuos sicut dies hesterna que preteriit et sicut custodia in nocte</foreign>.
89.5. Þa for nowihte beoð hæfd ger hyra <foreign>que pro nichilo habentur anni eorum</foreign>.
89.6. On morgynne swa swa wyrt leoryð on morgynne blowyð & þurhleoryð on æfyn gefeallyð forheardað & adruwað <foreign>Mane sicut herba transeat mane floreat et pertranseat uespere decidat induret et arescat</foreign>.
89.7. Forþon we asprungon on yrre þinum & on hatheortnysse þinre gedrefyde we synd <foreign>Quia defecimus in ira tua et in furore tuo conturbati sumus</foreign>.
89.8. Þu gesettyst unrihtwisnysse ure on gesihðe þinre worulde ure on onlyhtnysse andwlitan þinys <foreign>Posuisti iniquitates nostras in conspectu tuo seculum nostrum in inluminatione uultus tui</foreign>.
89.9. Forþon ealle dagas ure asprungon & we on yrre þinum asprungun gear ure swa swa wæfyrgange wæryn smeagynde <foreign>Quoniam omnes dies nostri defecerunt et nos in ira tua defecimus anni nostri sicut aranea meditabantur</foreign>.
89.10. Dægas geara ure on him hundseofuntig geara gif soðlice on mihtum his hundiehtatig gera & monigfealdum hyra geswinc & sar forþon ofyrcwon ofyr us manþwærnyss & we beoð gereafode <foreign>dies annorum nostrorum in ipsis lxx annis si autem in potentatibus eius lxxx anni et plurimum eorum labor et dolor quoniam superuenit super nos mansuetudo et corripiemur</foreign>.
89.11. Hwylc wat mihte yrrys þinys oððe for ege yrre þin <foreign>Quis nouit potestatem ire tue aut pre timore iram tuam</foreign>.
89.12. Atellan swiðre þin drihtyn cuð gedo us & gelærde on heortan on snotyrnysse <foreign>dinumerare dexteram tuam domine notam fac nobis et eruditos corde in sapientia</foreign>.
89.13. Gecyrr drihtyn sume hwile & bide beo þu ofyr þeowas ðine <foreign>Conuertere domine aliquantulum et deprecabilis esto super seruos tuos</foreign>.
89.14. Gefyllyde we syndon morgyne mildheortnysse þinre & we gefeoð & geblissode we synd on eallum dagum urum <foreign>Repleti sumus mane misericordia tua et exultauimus et delectati sumus in omnibus diebus nostris</foreign>.
89.15. Gelustfullude we synd for dagum þæt þu us geeaðmododyst gerum on þam we gesawyn yfyl <foreign>Delectati sumus pro digebus quibus nos humiliasti annis in quibus uidimus mala</foreign>.
89.16. Geloca on þeowas þine & on worca þin drihtyn & gerece bearn hyra <foreign>Respice in seruos tuos et in opera tua domine et dirige filios eorum</foreign>.
89.17. & sy beorhtnys drihtnys godys urys ofyr us & weorc handa ura gerece ofyr us & worc handa ura gerece <foreign>Et sit splendor domini dei nostri super nos et opera manuum nostrarum dirige super nos et opus manuum nostrarum dirige</foreign>.
90.1. Se eardað on fultume þæs heahstan on gescyldnysse godys hefynys wunað <foreign>Qvi habitat in adiutorio altissimi in protectione dei celi commorabitur</foreign>.
90.2. Cwyð to drihtne andfenga min eart þu & gebeorh min god min ic gehihte on hine <foreign>Dicet domino susceptor meus es et refugium meum deus meus sperabo in eum</foreign>.
90.3. Forþon he gefreoð me of gryne huntiyndra & fram worde grimmum <foreign>Quoniam ipse liberauit me de laqueo uenantium et a uerbo aspero</foreign>.
90.4. Mid gescyldrum his ofyrsceadwað þe & undyr fyðrum his þu gehihtyst <foreign>Scapulis suis obumbrabit tibi et su pennis eius sperabis</foreign>.
90.5. Mid scylde ymbsylyð þe soðfæstnyss his ne ondrædyst þu þe from ege nihtlicum <foreign>Scuto circumdabit te ueritas eius non timebis a timore nocturno</foreign>.
90.6. From flane fleogyndre þurh dæg fram ceapunge geondgangyndum on þystrum fram hryre & deofle middæglicum <foreign>a sagitta uolante per diem a negotio perambulante in tenebris a ruina et demonio meridiano</foreign>.
90.7. Feallað fram sidan þinre þusynd & tyn þusynd fram swiðran þinre þe soðlice na togenealæcyð <foreign>Cadent a latere tuo mille et decim milia a dextris tuis tibi autem non adpropiabit</foreign>.
90.8. Þeahhwæðere iegum þinum þu gesceawast & edlean synfullra þu gesihst <foreign>Uerumtamen oculis tuis considerabis et retributionem peccatorum uidebis</foreign>.
90.9. Forðon þu eart drihtyn hiht min hiehst þu gesettyst gebeorh þin <foreign>Quoniam tu es domine spes mea altissimum posuisti refugium tuum</foreign>.
90.10. Ne genealæcyn to þe yfyl & þreaung ne genealæcað getelde þinum <foreign>Non accedent ad te mala ac flagella non adpropiabunt tabernaculo tuo</foreign>.
90.11. Forþon englum his bebead be þe þæt hi heoldon þe on eallum wegum þinum <foreign>Quoniam angelis suis mandauit de te ut custodiant te in omnibus uiis tuis</foreign>.
90.12. On handum hi berað þe ne æfre þu oðspornyst to stane fot þin <foreign>In manibus protabunt te ne umquam offendas ad lapidem pedem tuum</foreign>.
90.13. Ofyr nædran & fagum wyrme þu gongyst & trydest leon & dracan <foreign>Super aspidem et basilliscum ambulabis et conculcabis leonem et draconem</foreign>.
90.14. Forþon on me gehihtyð ic alyse hine ic gescylde hine forþon he oncneow naman minne <foreign>Quoniam in me sperauit liberabo eum protegam eum quoniam cognouit nomen meum</foreign>.
90.15. Ingecigyþ me & ic gehyre hine mid hine ic eom on geswince ic generige hine & ic gewuldrige hine <foreign>Inuocauit me et ego exadiam eum cum ipso sum in tribulatione eripiam eum et glorificabo eum</foreign>.
90.16. Lenge daga ic gefylle hine & ic ætywe him hæle mine <foreign>longitudinem dierum adimplebo eum et ostendam illi salutare meum</foreign>.
91.2. God ys andyttan drihtyn & singan naman þinum þu hiehsta <foreign>Bonvm est confiteri domino et psallere nomini tuo altissime</foreign>.
91.3. To secgynne on morgynne mildheortnysse þine & soðfæstnysse þine þurh niht <foreign>Ad adnutiandum mane misericordiam tuam et ueritatem tuam per noctem</foreign>.
91.4. On tynstrengre hearpan mid canticsange & citran <foreign>In decachordo psalterio cum cantico et cythara</foreign>.
91.5. Forþon þu gelustfuludyst me drihtyn on worce þinum & on dædum handa þinra ic gefeo <foreign>quia delectasti me domine in factura tua et in operibus manuum tuarum exultabo</foreign>.
91.6. Hu micyllice synd worc þine drihtyn swiðe deope gewordyne synd geþohtas þine <foreign>Quam magnificata sunt opera tua domine nimis profunde facte sunt cogitatiiones tue</foreign>.
91.7. Wer unwis ne oncnæwð & dysig ne ongytyð þa <foreign>Vir insipiens non cognoscit et stultus non intellegit ea</foreign>.
91.8. Þonne upprynað þa synfullan swa swa heg & ætywdon ealle þa þe wyrcynde wæron unrihtwisnysse þæt forwyrðyð in woruld worulde <foreign>Cum exorientur peccatores sicut fenum et apparuerunt omnes qui operantur iniquitatem ut intereant in seculum seculi</foreign>.
91.9. Þu soðlice se hiehsta on ecnysse drihtyn <foreign>Tu autem altissimus in eternum domine</foreign>.
91.10. Forþon efnenu fynd þine drihtyn forwurðaþ & beoð tostrodynne ealle þa þe wyrceað unrihtwisnysse <foreign>Quoniam ecce inimici tui domine peribunt et dispergentur omnes qui operantur iniquitatem</foreign>.
91.11. & bið uppahafyn swa swa anhyrnys horn min & yld min on mildheortnysse genihtsumere <foreign>Et exaltabitur sicut unicornis cornu meum et senectus mea in misericordia uberi</foreign>.
91.12. & gelocode iege þin fynd min & arisynde on me wyrgynde gehyrde eare þin <foreign>Et respexit oculus tuus inimicos meos et in insurgentes in me malignantes audiuit auris tua</foreign>.
91.13. Se rihtwisa swa swa palmtwig blowyð & swa swa cedyrbeam þæs muntys bið gemonifealdod <foreign>Iustus ut palma florebit et sicut cedrus libani multiplicabitur</foreign>.
91.14. Geplantode on huse drihtnys on cafyrtune husys godys urys blowað <foreign>Plantate in domo domini in atriis domus dei nostri florebunt</foreign>.
91.15. Nugyt beoð gemonigfealdode on ylde genihtsumre & wel geþyldyge beoð <foreign>Adhuc multiplicabuntur in senecta uberi et bene patientes erunt</foreign>.
91.16. Þæt hi secgyn forþon rihtwis ys ys drihtyn god ure & nys unrihtwisnys on him <foreign>ut adnunient quoniam iustus est dominus deus noster et non est iniquitas in eo</foreign>.
92.1. Drihtyn rixað wlite gegyryð gegyryð drihtyn strenge & begyrdyð hine mid mægyne & soðlice he getrymyð ymbhwyrft eorðan se ðe ne byð onstyryd <foreign>Dominvs regnavit decorem induit induit dominus fortitudinem et precixit se uirtute etenim firmauit orbem terre qui non commouebitur</foreign>.
92.2. Gearwe setl þin god nu heonanforð fram worulde þu eart <foreign>Parata sedes tua deus ex tunc a seculo tu es</foreign>.
92.3. Upphofon flodas drihtyn uppahofon flodas stefne heora <foreign>Eleuauerunt flumina domine eleuauerunt flumina uoces suas</foreign>.
92.4. Fram stefnum wætra mænigra wundurlice upahafynysse sæys wundurlic on heannysse drihtyn <foreign>a uocibus aquarum multarum mirabiles elationes maris mirabilis in excelsis dominus</foreign>.
92.5. Cyðnyssa þina drihtyn geleaffulle gewordyne synd swiðe huse þinum gedafænað þan halgan drihtne on lenge daga <foreign>Testimonia tua domine credibilia facta sunt nimis domui tue decent sancta domine in longitudine dierum</foreign>.
93.1. God wreca drihtyn god wreca freolice dyde <foreign>Devs vltionvm dominus deus ultionum libere egit</foreign>.
93.2. Hefe upp þu þe demst eorðan agyld edlean ofyrhygdum <foreign>Exaltare qui iudicas terram redde retributionem superbis</foreign>.
93.3. Hu lange synfulle drihtyn hu lange synfulle beoð gewuldrude <foreign>Vsquequo peccatores domine usquequo peccatores gloriabuntur</foreign>.
93.4. Secgað & sprecað unrihtwisnysse sprecað ealle þa þe wyrceað unrihtwisnysse <foreign>Pronutiabunt et loquentur iniquitatem loquentur omnes qui operantur iniustitiam</foreign>.
93.5. Folc þin drihtyn geaðmeddon & yrfewyrdnysse þine geswætton <foreign>Populum tuum domine humiliauerunt et hereditatem tuam uexauerunt</foreign>.
93.6. Wydywan & wreccan ofslogon & fædyrlease ofslogon <foreign>Viduam et aduenam interfecerunt et pupillos occiderunt</foreign>.
93.7. & cwædon ne gesihþ drihtne ne ongyt god iacobys <foreign>Et dixerunt non uidebit dominus nec intellegit deus iacob</foreign>.
93.8. Ongytað nu þa þe unwise syndon on folce & dysige hwilum hogiað <foreign>Intellegite nunc qui insipientis estis in populo et stulti aliquando sapite</foreign>.
93.9. Se plantode eare ne gehyryð oþþe se ðe hiwude eage ne gesceawað <foreign>Qui plantauit aurem non audiet aut qui finxit oculum non considerat</foreign>.
93.10. Se þe þreað þeoda ne þreað se læryð mannan wisdom <foreign>qui corripit gentes non arguet qui docet hominem scientiam</foreign>.
93.11. Drihtyn wat geþohtas manna forþon idle hi synd <foreign>Dominus nouit cogitationes hominum quoniam uane sunt</foreign>.
93.12. Eadig mann þæne þu gelæryst drihtyn & of æ þinre þu gelærst hine <foreign>Beatus homo quem tu erudieris domine et de lege tua docueris eum</foreign>.
93.13. Þæt þu myðgie hine fram dagum yflvm oðþæt þe bið dolfyn þa synfullan scræf vel seaðe <foreign>ut mitiges eum a diebus malis donec fodeatur peccatori fouea</foreign>.
93.14. Forþon aweg ne adrifð drihtyn folc his & hyrfeweardnysse his ne forlætyð <foreign>Quia non repellet dominus plebem suam et hereditatem suam non derelinquet</foreign>.
93.15. Oðþæt rihtwisnys byþ gecyrryd on dom & þa nymað hi ealle þe rihtre synd heortan <foreign>Quoadusque iustitia conuertatur in iudicium et qui tenent eam omnes qui recto sunt corde</foreign>.
93.16. Hwylc arisyð me wið wyrgynde oððe hwilc stondyð mid me ongen wyrcynde unrihtwisnysse <foreign>Quis exurget mihi aduersus malignantes aut quis stabit mecum aduersus operantes iniquitatem</foreign>.
93.17. Nymþe forþon drihtyn gefultumode me hwene læssan eardode on helle sawle mine <foreign>Nisi quia dominus adiuuasset me paulo minus habitauerat in inferno anima meam</foreign>.
93.18. Gef ic cwæð onstyryd ys fot min mildheortnysse þin drihtyn gefultumað me <foreign>Si diecbam motus est pes meus misericordia tua domine adiuuabat me</foreign>.
93.19. Æftyr mænigeo sara minra on heortan minre frofre þine drihtyn geblissodon sawle mine <foreign>Secundum multitudinem dolorum meorum in corde meo consolationis tue domine letificauerunt animam meam</foreign>.
93.20. Ac genealæcð þe setl unrihtwisnysse heowæs sar on bybode <foreign>Numquid adheret tibi sedes iniquitatis qui fingis dolorem in precepto</foreign>.
93.21. Gehæftað on sawle þæs rihtwisan & blod unsceðþyndra hi genyðriað <foreign>captabunt in animam iusti et sanguinem innocentem condemnabunt</foreign>.
93.22. & gewordyn ys me drihtyn on gebeorh & god min on fultum hihtys minys <foreign>Et factus est mihi dominus in refugium et deus meus in auxilium spei meae</foreign>.
93.23. & gyldyð him drihtyn god unrihtwisnysse heora & on yfylsacunge heoræ tostregdyð hi drihtyn god ure <foreign>Et reddet illis dominus deus iniquitates ipsorum et in malitiis eorum disperdet illos dominus deus noster</foreign>.
94.1. Cumað gefeon we drihtne wynsumiyn we gode þan halwendan urum <foreign>Venite exvltemus domino iubilemus deo salutari nostro</foreign>.
94.2. Abysgiyn we onsyne his on andytnysse & on sealmum wynsumiyn we him <foreign>Preocupemus faciem eius in confessione et in psalmis iubilemus ei</foreign>.
94.3. Forþon god micyl drihtyn & cing micyl ofyr ealle godas forþan onweg ne adrifð drihtyn folc his <foreign>Quoniam deus magnus dominus et rex magnus super omnes deos quoniam non repellet dominus plebem suam</foreign>.
94.4. Forþon on handa his synd ealle endas eorðan & heanysse munta he gelocað <foreign>quia in manu eius sunt omnes fines terre et altitudines montium ipse conspicit</foreign>.
94.5. Forþon his ys sæ & he dyde þæt & þa drigean gestaþolodan handa his <foreign>Quoniam ipsius est mare et ipse fecit illud et aridam fundauerunt manus eius</foreign>.
94.6. Cumað we weorðiyn & forðlutun we beforan gode wepyn we beforan drihtne se ðe geworhte us <foreign>Venite adoremus et procidamus ante deum ploremus coram domino qui fecit nos</foreign>.
94.7. Forþon he ys drihtyn god ure us soðlice folc his & sciep læswe his <foreign>Quia ipse est dominus deus noster nos autem populus eius et oues pascue eius</foreign>.
94.8. To dæge gef stefne his ge gehyrað nellad ge geheardian heortan eowre <foreign>Hodie si uocem eius audieritsi nolite obdurare corda uestra</foreign>.
94.9. Swa swa on onscununge æftyr dæge costunge on westynne þær costodon me fædras eowre fandodan vel cunnydon & gesawon worc min <foreign>Sicut in exacerbatione secundum diem temptationis in deserto ubi temptauerut me patres uestri probauerunt et uiderunt opera mea</foreign>.
94.10. Feowyrtigum geara on neawyste ic wæs cneorysse þisse & ic cwæð symle ðas dwoliað heortan <foreign>Quadraginta annis proximus fui generationi huic et dixi semper hii errant corde</foreign>.
94.11. Hy soðlice ne oncneowon wegas mine þam ic swor on yrre minum gef hi inngað on reste minre <foreign>Ipsi uero non cognouerunt uias meas quibus iuraui inn ira mea si introibunt in requiem meam</foreign>.
95.1. Singað drihtne sang niwne singað drihtne eall eorðe <foreign>Cantate domino canticum nouum cantate domino omnis terra</foreign>.
95.2. Singað drihtne & bledsiað naman his wel secgað of dæge on dæg hæle his <foreign>Cantate domino et benedicite nomini eius bene nuntiate de die in diem salutare eius</foreign>.
95.3. Secgað betwyh þeodum wuldor his on eallum folcum wundur his <foreign>Adnuntiate inter gentes gloriam eius in omnibus populis mirabilia eius</foreign>.
95.4. Forþon micyl drihtyn & hergendlic swiðe egysfull ofyr ealle goda <foreign>Quoniam magnus dominus et laudabilis nimis terribilis est super omnes deos</foreign>.
95.5. Forþon ealle godas þeoda deofol drihtyn soðlice hefonas dyde <foreign>Quoniam omnes dii gentium demonia dominus autem celos fecit</foreign>.
95.6. Andytnyss & fægyrnys on gesihðe his halignys & micylnys on gehalgunge his <foreign>Confessio et pulchritudo in conspectu eius sanctitas et magnificentia in sanctificatione eius</foreign>.
95.7. Tobringað drihtne oeðleas þeoda tobringað drihtne wuldur & are <foreign>Adferte domino patrie gentium adferte domino gloriam et honorem</foreign>.
95.8. Bringað drihtne wuldor naman his uphebbað onsægdnysse & inngað on cafyrtunas his <foreign>adferte domino gloriam nomine eius tollite hostias et introite in atria eius</foreign>.
95.9. Wurþiað drihtyn on healle þære halgan his sy onstyryd fram ansyne his eall eorðe <foreign>adhorate dominum in in aula sancta eius commoueatur a facie eius uniuersa terra</foreign>.
95.10. Cweðað on cneoryssum drihtyn ricsað fram treowe & soðlice gerecyð ymbhwyrft eorðan se ne bið onstyryd demyð folc unrihtwisnysse & þeoda on yrre his <foreign>dicite inationibus dominus regnauit a ligno etenim correxit orbem terre qui non commouebitur iudicabit populos in equitate et gentes in ira sua</foreign>.
95.11. Blissiyn hefonas & gefeo eorðe sy onstyryd sæ & gefyllydnys hyre <foreign>Letentur celi et exultet terra moueatur mare et plenitudo eius</foreign>.
95.12. Gefeoð feldas & ealle þa þe on him synd þonne gefeoð ealle treowu wuda <foreign>Gaudebunt campi et omnia que in ei sunt tunc exultabunt omnia ligna siluarum</foreign>.
95.13. Beforan ansyne drihtnys forþan cwom forþan cwom to demanne eorðan he demð ymbhwyrft eorðan on efynnysse & folc on soðfæstnysse his <foreign>ante faciem domini quoniam uenit quoniam uenit iudicare terram iudicabit orbem terre in equitate et populos in ueritate sua</foreign>.
96.1. Drihtyn ricsað gefehð eorðan blissiyn ealand micyle <foreign>Dominvs regnavit exultet terra letentur insule multe</foreign>.
96.2. Wolcyn & dymnys on ymbhwyrfte his rihtwisnys & dom gerecnyss setlys his <foreign>Nubes et caligo in circuitu eius iustitia et iudicium correctio sedes eius</foreign>.
96.3. Fyr beforan him foregæð & onælyð on ymbhwyrfte fynd his <foreign>Ignis ante eum preibit et inflammabit in circuitu inimicos eius</foreign>.
96.4. Onlihtun ligytto his ymbhwyrfte eorðan geseah & onstyryd wæs eorðe <foreign>Inluxerunt fulgora eius orbi terre uidit et commota est terra</foreign>.
96.5. Muntas swa swa wiex toflowyn from ansyne drihtnys fram ansyne drihtnys cwacude eall eorðe <foreign>Montes sicut cera fluxerunt a facie domini a facie domini tremuit omnis terra</foreign>.
96.6. Sægdon hefonas rihtwisnysse his & gesawon ealle folc wuldor his <foreign>Adnuntiauerunt celi iustitiam eius et uiderunt omnes populi gloriam eius</foreign>.
96.7. Syn gescynde ealle þa þe wurðiað græftys & þa þe wuldriað on hergum his wurðiað hine ealle englas his <foreign>Confundantur omnes qui adhorant sculptilia et qui gloriantur in simulacris suis adorate eum omnes angeli eius</foreign>.
96.8. Gehyrde & geblissod ys sion & gefægon dohtra iudan for domum þinum drihtne <foreign>audiuit et letata est sion et exultauerunt filie iude propter iudicia tua domine</foreign>.
96.9. Forðon þu eart drihtyn heahsta ofyr ealle eorðan swiðe upahafyn is ofyr ealle godas <foreign>Quoniam tu est dominus altissimus super omnem terram nimis exaltatus es super omnes deos</foreign>.
96.10. Þa þe lufiað drihtyn feogeað yfyl healdyð drihtyn sawla þeowa his of handa synfulra gefreoð hi <foreign>Qui diligitis dominum odite malum custodit dominus animas seruorum suorum de manu peccatorum liberabit eos</foreign>.
96.11. Leoht upcumyn ys þam rihtan & rihtheortan blissie <foreign>Lux orta est iusto et rectis corde letitia</foreign>.
96.12. Blissiað rihtwise on drihtyn & andyttað gemynde halignysse his <foreign>letamini iusti in domino et confitemini memorie sanctitatis eius</foreign>.
97.1. Singað drihtne sang niwne forþon wundur dyde drihtyn gehælde hine swiðre his & earm haligne his <foreign>Cantate domino canticum nouum quia mirabilia fecit dominus saluabit sibi dexteram eius et brachium sanctum eius</foreign>.
97.2. Cuðe dyde drihtyn hæle his beforan gesihðe þeoda onwrieh rihtwisnysse his <foreign>Notum fecit dominus salutare suum ante conspectu gentium reuelauit iustitiam suam</foreign>.
97.3. Gemyndig wæs mildheortnysse his iacobys & soðfæstnysse his gehusscype irahelys gesawon ealle endas eorðan hæle godys urys <foreign>Memor fuit misericordie sue iacob et ueritatis sue domui israhel viderunt omnes fines terre salutare dei nostri</foreign>.
97.4. Wynsumiað gode ælc eorðe singað & gefeoð & singað <foreign>iubilate deo omnis terra cantate et exultate et psallite</foreign>.
97.5. Singað gode urum on citran on citran & stefne sealmys <foreign>Psallite deo nostro in cythara in cythara et uoce psalmi</foreign>.
97.6. On hornum gelengdum & stefne hornys hyrnys wvnsumiað on gesihðe cyningys drihtnys <foreign>in tubis ductilibus et uoce tube corneae iubilate in conspectu regis domino</foreign>.
97.7. Sy onstyryd sæ & fullnys his ymbhwyrft eorðan & ealle þa þe eardiað on hyre <foreign>Moueatur mare et plenitudo eius orbis terrarum et uniuersi qui habitant in eo</foreign>.
97.8. Flodas plegiað handum on þæt ilce muntas gefengvn <foreign>Flumina plaudent manibus in id ipsum montes exultauerunt</foreign>.
97.9. Beforan ansyne drihtnys forþon cwom forþon cwom deman eorðan demyð ymbhwyrft eorðan on riht & folc on efynnysse <foreign>ante faciem domini quoniam uenit quoniam uenit iudicare terram iudicabit orbem terre in iustitia et populos in equitate</foreign>.
98.1. Drihtyn ricsað yrsiyn folce þu þe sityst ofyr cherubin sy onstyryd eorðe <foreign>Dominvs regnavit irascantur populi qui sedes super cherubin moueatur terra</foreign>.
98.2. Drihtyn on sion micyl & hieh ofyr ealle folc <foreign>Dominus in sion magnus et excelsus super omnes populos</foreign>.
98.3. Andyttað naman þinum micyl & egesfullum forþon halig ys <foreign>Confiteantur nomini tuo magno et terribilis quonia sanctum est</foreign>.
98.4. & are cyningys dom lufað þu gegearwodyst rihtwisnysse dom & rihtwisnysse on iacob þu dydyst <foreign>et honor regis iudicium diligit tu parasti equitatem iudicium et iustitiam in iacob tu fecisti</foreign>.
98.5. Upahebbað drihtyn god ure & wurðiað scamul fota his forþon halig ys <foreign>Exaltate dominum deum nostrum et adorate scabellum pedum eius quoniam sanctum est</foreign>.
98.6. Moyses & aaron on sacerdum his & samuel betwuh hi þa þe gecigeað naman his <foreign>Moyses et aaron in sacerdotibus eius et samuel inter eos qui inuocant nomen eius inuocabant dominum et ipse exaudiebat eos</foreign>.
98.7. On syle vel on swer wolcnys spræc to him heoldon cyðnysse his & bebod his þa he sealde him <foreign>in columna nubis loquebatur ad eos custodiebant testimonia eius et precepta eius que dederat illis</foreign>.
98.8. Drihtyn god ure þu gehyrdyst hi god þu milde wære him & wrecynde on ealle tylunga hyra <foreign>Domine deus noster tu exaudiebas eos deus tu propicius fuisti illis et uindicans in omnia studia eorum</foreign>.
98.9. Hebbað upp drihtyn god ure & wurðiað on munte halgum his forþon halig ys drihtyn god ure <foreign>Exaltate dominum deum nostrum et adorate in monte sancto eius quoniam sanctus est dominus deus noster</foreign>.
99.2. Wynsumiað gode eall eorðe þeowiað drihtne on blisse ingað on gesihðe his on wynsumnysse <foreign>Ivbilate deo omnis terra seruite domino in letitia intrate in conspectu eius in exultatione</foreign>.
99.3. Witað ge þæt drihtyn he ys god he worhte us & nalys we usic we soðlice folc his & scep læswe his <foreign>scitote quod dominus ipse est deus ipse fecit nos et non ipsi nos nos autem populus eius et oues pascue eius</foreign>.
99.4. Ingað gatu his on andytnysse cafyrtunys his on ymenum andyttnysse hergeað naman his <foreign>intrate portas eius in confessione atria eius in ymnys confessionum laudate nomen eius</foreign>.
99.5. Forþon wynsum ys drihtyn on ecnysse mildheortnysse his & oð on woruld worulde soðfæstnysse his <foreign>quoniam suauis est dominus in eternum misericordia eius et usque in seculum seculi ueritas eius</foreign>.
100.1. Mildheortnysse & dom ic singe þe drihtyn ic singe <foreign>Misericordiam et iudicium cantabo tibi domine psallam</foreign>.
100.2. & ic ongyte on wege þæs unwemman þonne þu cymyst to me ic geondgange on unsceðfulnysse heortan minre on midle husys þinys <foreign>et intellegam in uia inmaculata quando uenies ad me perambulabam in innocentia cordis mei in medio domus tue</foreign>.
100.3. No ic foresette beforan eagum minum wisan yfyle doynde ofyrleornysse ic feode & ne ætfealh me <foreign>Non proponebam ante oculos meos rem malam facientes preuaricationis odiui et non adhesit mihi</foreign>.
100.4. Heorte þweorh onhyldynde fram me awyrgynde ic ne oncnew <foreign>cor prauum declinantes a me malignos non agnoscebam</foreign>.
100.5. Gelendne wið þam niehstan his digyllice þisne ic iehte ofyrhidgum eagum & ungereodlicre heortan mid þis samod ic ne æt <foreign>detrahentem aduersus proximum suum occulte hunc persequebar superbo oculo et insatabili corde cum hoc simul non edebam</foreign>.
100.6. Egan mine ofyr þa getreowe eorðan þæt hi sittun þæs mid me gongynde on wege þam unwemman þes me þegnað <foreign>Oculi mei super fideles terre ut sedeant hii mecum ambulans in uia inmaculata hic mihi ministrabat</foreign>.
100.7. Ne eardæð on midle huss minys se deð ofyrhygde & se sprecð þam unrihtan ne gerecð on gesihðe iegyna minra <foreign>Non habitabit in medio domus mee qui facit superbiam et qui loquitur iniqua non dirigetur in conspectu oculorum meorum</foreign>.
100.8. On morgyntid ic ofsloh ealle synfulle eorðe þæt ic tostregde of ciestre drihtnys ealle wyrceað unrihtwisnysse <foreign>In matutinis interficiebam omnes peccatores terre ut disperdam de ciuitate domini omnes qui operantur iniquitatem</foreign>.
101.2. Drihten gehyr gebed min & clypung min to þe becumað <foreign>Domine exavdi orationem meam et clamor meus ad te perueniat</foreign>.
101.3. Ne acyr þu onsyne þine fram me on swa hwylcum dæge ic beom geswencyd onhyld to me eare þin on swa hwylcum dæge ic gehyre þe hrædlice gehyr me <foreign>Ne auertas faciem tuam a me in quacumque die tribulor inclina ad me aurem tuam in quacumque die inuocauero te uelociter exaudi me</foreign>.
101.4. Forþon asprungyn swa swa smic dagas mine & ban mine swa swa on hyrstepannan gehyrste synd <foreign>Quia defecerunt sicut fumus dies mei et ossa mea sicut in frixorio confrixa sunt</foreign>.
101.5. Ofslegyn ic eom swa swa heg & adruwað heorte min forðan ofyrgytyl ic eom etan hlaf minne <foreign>Percussus sum sicut fenum et aruit cor meum quia oblitus sum manducare panem meum</foreign>.
101.6. Fram stefne geomrunge mine genealæhte ban minum flæsce minum <foreign>a uoce gemitus mei adheserunt ossa mea carni mee</foreign>.
101.7. Gelice gewordyn ic eom stangyllan on westynne gewordyn ic eom swa swa nihthræfn on husiycyle <foreign>Similis factus sum pellicano in solitudine factus sum sicut nicticorax in domicilio</foreign>.
101.8. Ic wacode & gewordyn ic eom swa swa spearwa se anga on timbre <foreign>uigilaui et factus sum sicut passer unicus in edificio</foreign>.
101.9. Ealne dæg oðwiton me fynd mine & þa þe me hergeað ongen me sworon <foreign>Tota die exprobrabant me inimici mei et qui me laudabant aduersum me iurabant</foreign>.
101.10. Forþon ahsan swa swa hlaf ic æt & drenc minne mid wope ic gemetgode <foreign>Quia cinerem sicut panem manducabam et potum meum cum fletu temperabam</foreign>.
101.11. Fram onsyne yrre æbyligþu þinre forþon uppahebbynd þu gecnysydys me <foreign>a facie ire indignationis tue quia eleuans allisisti me</foreign>.
101.12. Dagas mine swa swa sceadu onhyldon & ic swa swa hig adruwode <foreign>Dies mei sicut umbra declinauerunt et ego sicut fenum arui</foreign>.
101.13. Þu soðlice drihtyn on ecnysse þurhwunast & gemynd þin on woruld worulde <foreign>Tu autem domine in eternum permanes et memoriale tuum in seculum seculi</foreign>.
101.14. Þu arisynde drihtyn þu gemiltsast syon forþon cwom tid to myltsiynde his <foreign>Tu exsurgens domine misereberis sion quia uenit tempus miserendi eius</foreign>.
101.15. Forþon welgelicod hæfdon þeowys þinys stanys his & eorþe his mildsiað <foreign>Quia beneplacitos habuerunt serui tui lapides eius et terre eius miserebuntur</foreign>.
101.16. & ondrædað þeoda naman þinne drihtyn & ealle cyningas eorðan wuldur þin <foreign>Et timebunt gentes nomen tuum domine et omnes reges terre gloriam tuam</foreign>.
101.17. Forþan timbryð drihtyn syon & bið gesewyn on mægynðrymme his <foreign>Quoniam edificauit dominus sion et uidebitur in maiestate sua</foreign>.
101.18. & gelocað on gebedu þearfyna & ne forhogað bena hyra <foreign>Et respexit in orationes pauperum et non spreuit preces eorum</foreign>.
101.19. Beoð awrityn þas on cneorysse oðyrre & folc þæt bið gecwicod heryð drihtyn <foreign>Scribantur hec in generatione altera et populus qui creabitur laudabit dominum</foreign>.
101.20. Forðon gelocað of heannysse halgan his drihtyn of hefone on eorðan gelocode <foreign>Quoniam prospexit de excelso sancto suo dominus de celo in terram prospexit</foreign>.
101.21. Þæt he gehyrde geomrunge gebundynra þæt he onlyse bearn ofslegynra <foreign>Ut audiret gemitum uinculatorum ut soluat filios interemptorum</foreign>.
101.22. Þæt sy sægd on sion naman drihtnys & lof his on hierusalem <foreign>Vt adnuntietur in sion nomen domini et laus eius in hierusalem</foreign>.
101.23. On gemetinge folca on annysse & ricu þæt hi þeowiyn drihtne <foreign>In conueniendo populos in unum et regna ut seruiant domino</foreign>.
101.24. Geandswarode him on wege mægnys his sceortnysse daga minra sege me & <foreign>Respondit ei in uia uirtutis sue paucitatem dierum meorum enuntia mihi et</foreign>.
101.25. Ne gecigst þu me on midle daga minra on woruld worulde gerys þinys <foreign>ne reuoces me in dimedio dierum meorum in seculum seculi anni tui</foreign>.
101.26. On fruman eorðan þu gestaþolodyst drihtyn & worc handa þinra synd hefonys <foreign>Initio terram tu fundasti domine et opera manuum tuarum sunt celi</foreign>.
101.27. Hi forwurðað þu soðlice þurhwunast & ealle swa swa hrægl ealdiað & swa swa ofyrwrigyls þu onwendyst hi & hi beoð onwendyd <foreign>Ipsi peribunt tu autem permanebis et omnia sicut uestimentum ueterescent et sicut opertorium mutabis eos et mutabuntur</foreign>.
101.28. Þu soðlice se ylca iert & ger þine ne ateoriað <foreign>Tu autem idem ipse es et anni tui non deficient</foreign>.
101.29. Bearn þeowa þinra oneardiað þær & sæd hyra on woruld worulde bið gereht <foreign>Filii seruorum tuorum inhabitabunt ibi et semen eorum in seculum seculi dirigetur</foreign>.
102.1. Bledsa sawle mine drihtyn & ealle ða innyran mine naman þone halgan his <foreign>Benedic anima mea dominum et omnia interiora mea nomen sanctum eius</foreign>.
102.2. Bledsa sawle mine drihtne & nelle þu ofyrgytan ealle edlean his <foreign>Benedic anima mea dominum et noli obliuisci omnes retributiones eius</foreign>.
102.3. Se arfull vel milde bið eallum unrihtwisnyssum þinum se hælyð ealle adla þine <foreign>Qui propitiatur omnibus iniquitatibus tuis qui sanat omnes languores tuos</foreign>.
102.4. Se alysyð of forwyrde lif þin <foreign>Qui redemit de interitu uitam tuam</foreign>.
102.5. Se gefyllyð on godum lust vel gewilnunge þine se gebeagað þe on myldse & mildheortnysse bið geedniwod swa swa earn iuguð þin <foreign>qui satiat in bonis desiderium tuum qui coronat te in miseratione et misericordia renouabitur sicut aquile iuunetus tua</foreign>.
102.6. Doynde mildheortnyssa drihtyn & dom eallum teonan þrowiyndum <foreign>Faciens misericordias dominus et iudicium omnibus iniuriam patientibus</foreign>.
102.7. Cvðe he dyde wegas his moisi bearn israhel willan his <foreign>Notas fecit uias suas moysi filiis israhel uoluntates suas</foreign>.
102.8. Mildheort & miltsiynd drihtyn geþyldig & swiðe mildheort <foreign>Misericors et miserator dominus patiens ut multum misericors</foreign>.
102.9. Nalys on ende yrsað ne on ecnysse bið geæbylgyd <foreign>Non in finem irascetur neque in eternum indignabitur</foreign>.
102.10. Nælys æftyr synnum urum he dyde us ne æftyr unrihtwisnyssum urum geedleanað us <foreign>Non secundum peccata nostra fecit nobis neque secundum iniquitates nostras retribuit nobis</foreign>.
102.11. Forþon æftyr heanysse hefonys & eorðe getrymyde drihtyn mildheortnysse hys ofyr ondrædynde hyne <foreign>Quia secundum altitudinem celi a terra confirmauit dominus misericordiam suam super timentes eum</foreign>.
102.12. Swa mycyl tostondyð eastdæl fram westdæle afeorrað fram us rihtwisnysse ure <foreign>Quamtum distat oriens ab occasu elongauit a nobis iniquitates nostras</foreign>.
102.13. Swa swa myldsað fædyr his bearnum swa mildsiynd ys drihtyn ondrædynde hine <foreign>Sicut miseretur pater filiis ita misertus est dominus timentibus se</foreign>.
102.14. Forðan he wat gehiwunge vel brogedetunge ure gemyne drihtyn þæt dust we synd <foreign>quia ipse scit figmentum nostrum memento domine quod puluis sumus</foreign>.
102.15. Mann swa swa heg dagas his swa swa blostma landys swa blowyð <foreign>homo sicut fenum dies eius sicut flos agri ita florebit</foreign>.
102.16. Forþon gast þurhleoryð fram him & ne bið & ne oncnæwð ma stowe his <foreign>Quia spiritus pertransiuit ab eo et non erit et non cognoscet amplius locum suum</foreign>.
102.17. Mildheortnys soðlice drihtnys fram worulde ys & oð on woruld worulde ofyr ondrædynde hine & rihtwisnyss his ofyr bearn bearna <foreign>Misericordia autem domini a seculo est et usque in seculum seculi super timentes eum et iustitia eius super filios filiorum</foreign>.
102.18. Healdyndum cyðnysse his & gemynd nymyndum bebodu his þæt don þæt <foreign>custodientibus testamentum eius et memoria retinentibus mandata eius ut faciant ea</foreign>.
102.19. Drihtyn on hefone gegearwude setl his & rice his ealra wealdyð <foreign>Dominus in celo parauit sedem suam et regnum eius omnium dominabitur</foreign>.
102.20. Bledsiað drihtyn ealle englas his mihtige on mægne þa þe doþ word his to gehyranne stefne worda his <foreign>Benedicite dominum omnes angeli eius potentes uirtute qui facitis uerbum eius ad audiendam uocem sermonum eius</foreign>.
102.21. Bledsiað drihtyn ealle mægnu his & þenas his þe doð willan his <foreign>Benedicite dominum omnes uirtutes eius et ministri eius qui facitis uoluntatem eius</foreign>.
102.22. Bledsiað drihtyn ealle worc his on ælcre stowe onwealdys his bledsa sawle mine drihtyn <foreign>Benedicite dominum omnia opera eius in omni loco dominationis eius benedic anima mea dominum</foreign>.
103.1. Bledsa sawle mine drihtyn drihtyn god min gemiclod eart swiðlice andytnysse & wlite þu gegyrydyst <foreign>Benedic anima mea dominum domine deus meus magnificatus es uehementer confessionem et decorem induisti</foreign>.
103.2. Beswapyn leohte swa swa mid hrægle aþeniynde hefyn swa swa fell <foreign>amictus lumine sicut uestimento extendens celum sicut pellem</foreign>.
103.3. Ðu þe beþecyst on wætrum þa ufyrran his se setyð wolcn uppstige his se gæð ofyr fiðru winda <foreign>qui tegis in aquis superiora eius qui ponit nubem ascensum suum qui ambulat super pennas uentorum</foreign>.
103.4. Se deð englas his gast & þegnas his fyr byrnynde <foreign>Qui facit angelos suos spiritus et ministros suos ignem urentem</foreign>.
103.5. Se staðolode eorðan ofyr staðolfæstnysse his ne bið onhyldyd on woruld worulde <foreign>Qui fundauit terram super stabilitatem eius non inclinabitur in seculum seculi</foreign>.
103.6. Nywolnyss swa swa ryft swæpyls his ofyr muntas standað wætyr <foreign>Abissus sicut pallium amictus eius super montes stabunt aque</foreign>.
103.7. Fra þreaunge þinre fleoð from stefne þunorrade þinre forhtiað <foreign>Ab increpatione tua fugient a uocem tonitrui tui formidabunt</foreign>.
103.8. Upastigað muntas & niðyrastigað feldas on stowe þæne gestaðolodyst him <foreign>Ascendunt montes et descendunt campi in locum quem fundasti eis</foreign>.
103.9. Gemære þu gesettyst him þæt hi ne ofyrgangaþ ne ne beoð forcyrryde ofyrwreon eorðan <foreign>terminum posuisti eis quem non transgredientur neque conuertentur operire terram</foreign>.
103.10. Se onsendyþ wyllas on dælum betux middyl munta þurhleorað vel farað wætyr <foreign>Qui emittit fontes in conuallibus inter medium montium pertransibunt aque</foreign>.
103.11. Drenceað þa ealle wildeor wuda bidað wilde assan on þurste hira <foreign>Potabunt ea omnes bestie siluarum expectabunt onagri in siti sua</foreign>.
103.12. Ofyr þa fuglas hefonas eardiað of midle stana syllað stefne his <foreign>super ea uolucres celi habitabunt de medio petrarum dabunt uoces suas</foreign>.
103.13. Leccynde muntas of þam ofyrrum his of wæstme worca þinra bið gefyllyd eorðe <foreign>Rigans montes de superioribus suis de fructu operum tuorum satiabitur terra</foreign>.
103.14. Forð lædynde heg neatum & wyrte to þeowdome manna þæt he utalæde hlaf of eorðan <foreign>Producens fenum iumentis et herbam seruituti hominum vt educat panem de terra</foreign>.
103.15. & win geblissað heortan mannys þæt he gladie onsyne on ele & hlaf heortan mannys getrymyð <foreign>et uinum letificet cor homines ut exilarit faciem in oleo et panis cor hominis confirmet</foreign>.
103.16. Beoð gefyllyde ealle treowu wudu & cedyrbeamas þæs muntys þa þu geplantodyst <foreign>Satiabuntur omnia ligna siluarum et cedri libani quas plantasti</foreign>.
103.17. Þær spearwan nystað hafocys hvs ladteow ys hyra <foreign>illic passeres nidificabunt fulice domus dux est eorum</foreign>.
103.18. Muntas hiehe heortys stan gebeorh ilys <foreign>montes excelsi ceruis petra refugium herinacis</foreign>.
103.19. He worhte sunnan on tide sunne oncneow setlgang hyra <foreign>Fecit lunam in tempore sol cognouit occasum suum</foreign>.
103.20. Þu settyst þystru & gewordys ys niht on hiræ þurhfarað ealle wildeor wuda <foreign>Posuisti tenebras et facta est nox in ipsa pertransibunt omnes bestie siluarum</foreign>.
103.21. Hwelpas leona grymytigynde þæt hi reafiyn & secyn from gode mete him <foreign>Catuli leonum rugientes ut rapiant et querant a deo escam sibi</foreign>.
103.22. Upcumyn ys sunne & gesomnode synd & on gebedclyfan hyra hi hi gestaðliað <foreign>Ortus est sol et congregati sunt et in cubilibus suis se collocabunt</foreign>.
103.23. Utgæð man to worce his & to gebede his oð æfyn <foreign>Exiet homo ad hopus suum et ad operationem suam usque ad uesperum</foreign>.
103.24. Hu micyllice synd worc þin drihtyn ealle on snyttro þu geworhtys gefyllyd ys eorðe gesceafta þinra <foreign>Quam magnificata sunt opera tua domine omnia in sapientia fecisti repleta est terra creatura tua</foreign>.
103.25. Þeos sæ micyl & rum þær slincynde þara nys nan gerim nietynu lytle & micle <foreign>Hoc mare magnum et spatiosum illic reptilia quorum non est numerus animalia pusilla et magna</foreign>.
103.26. Þær scypu þurhfarað draca þes þone þu gehiwodyst to bysmriynne him <foreign>illic naues pertransibunt draco iste quem formasti ad inludendum ei</foreign>.
103.27. Ealle from þe bidað drihtyn þæt þu sylle him mete on tid <foreign>omnia a te expectant domine ut des illis escam in tempore</foreign>.
103.28. Syllynde þe him gesomniað ontynyndum þe hand þine ealle beoð gefullyde genihtsumnysse <foreign>Dante te illis colligent aperiente te manum tuam omnia replebuntur ubertate</foreign>.
103.29. Fromcyrrynde soðlice þe onsyne þine beoþ gedrefyde þu afyrryst gast hyra & hi ateoriað & on hyra hi eftgecyrrað <foreign>Auertente autem te faciem tuam turbabuntur aufers spiritum eorum et deficient et in puluerem suum reuertentur</foreign>.
103.30. Asend gast þinne & hi beoð gecwicude & þu geedniwast onsyne eorðan <foreign>Emitte spiritum tuum et creabuntur et renouabis faciem terre</foreign>.
103.31. Sy wuldur drihtnys on woruld worulde bið geblissod drihtyn on worcum his <foreign>Sit gloria domini in seculum seculi letabitur dominus in operibus suis</foreign>.
103.32. Se gelocað on eorðan & deþ hi byfgean se gehrinð muntas & smeocað <foreign>Qui respicit in terram et facit eam tremere qui tangit montes et fumigabunt</foreign>.
103.33. Ic singe drihtne on life minum ic singe gode minum swa lange swa ic beo <foreign>Cantabo domino in uita mea psallam deo meo quamdiu ero</foreign>.
103.34. Wynsum sy him herynyss min ic soðlice beon gelustfullod on drihtne <foreign>Suauis sit ei laudatio mea ego uero delectabor in domino</foreign>.
103.35. Aspringað synfulle fram eorðan & unrihtwise swa þæt hine synd bledsa sawle mine drihtyn <foreign>Deficiant peccatores a terra et iniqui ita ut non sint benedic anima mea dominum</foreign>.
104.1. Drihtyn & gecigeað naman his secgað betwuh þeoda worc his <foreign>Confitemini domino et inuocate nomen eius adnuntiate inter gentes opera eius</foreign>.
104.2. Singað him & singað secgað ealle wundor his <foreign>Cantate ei et psallite narrate omnia mirabilia eius</foreign>.
104.3. Hergeað on naman halgan his blissiað heorte secyndra drihtyn <foreign>Laudamini in nomine sancto eius letetur cor querentium dominum</foreign>.
104.4. Seceað drihtyn & beoð getrymyde seceað onsyne his symle <foreign>Querite dominum et confirmamini querite faciem eius semper</foreign>.
104.5. Gemunað wundra his þa he dyde forebiec & dom muðys his <foreign>Mementote mirabilium eius que fecit prodigia et iudicia oris eius</foreign>.
104.6. Sæd abrahamys þeowys his bearn iacobys gecoryn his <foreign>Semen abrahe serui eius filii iacob electi eius</foreign>.
104.7. He drihtyn god ure on ealre eorðan dom his <foreign>Ipse dominus deus noster in uniuersa terra iudicia eius</foreign>.
104.8. Gemyndig wæs on woruld cyðnysse his wordys þæt he bebead on þusyn cneoryssa <foreign>Memor fuit in seculum testamenti sui uerbi quod mandauit in mille generationes</foreign>.
104.9. Þæt gestihtode to abraham & aðstæf his to isaac <foreign>Quod disposuit ad abraham et iuramenti sui ad isaac</foreign>.
104.10. & gesette þæt on bebod & israhel on cyðnysse ece <foreign>et statuit illud iacob in preceptum et israel in testamentum eternum</foreign>.
104.11. Cweðynde þe ic sylle eorðan rap yrfys eowrys <foreign>Dicens tibi dabo terram chanaan funiculum hereditatis uestre</foreign>.
104.12. Midþi hi wæron on gerime sceortum þa feawystan & landleode on him <foreign>Cum essent in numero breui paucissimi et incole in ea</foreign>.
104.13. & þurhferdon of þeode on þeode & of rice to folce oðrum <foreign>et pertransierunt de gente in gentem et de regno ad populum alterum</foreign>.
104.14. Ne forlet mann sceþþan him & þreade for him cynyngas <foreign>Non permisit hominem nocere eis et corripuit pro eis reges</foreign>.
104.15. Nyllyn ge æthrinan þa gehalgedan mine & on witegan minum nellyn ge wyrgean <foreign>Nolite tangere cristus meos et in prophetis meis nolite malignari</foreign>.
104.16. & he gecigde hungur ofyr eorðan & ealle trymenysse hlafys forþræste <foreign>Et uocauit famen super terram et omne firmamentum panis contriuit</foreign>.
104.17. Sende beforan hi wer on þeow beboht wæs ioseph <foreign>Misit ante eos uirum in seruum uenundatus est ioseph</foreign>.
104.18. Geeaðmeddun & gehyndon on fotcospum fet his isyn þurhferde sawl his <foreign>humiliauerunt in conpedibus pedes eius ferrum pertransiuit animam eius</foreign>.
104.19. Oðþæt cwome word hys gespræc drihtnys onlegeodon hyne <foreign>donec ueniret uerbum eius eloquium domini inflammauit eum</foreign>.
104.20. Sende cyning & onlysde hine ealdormann folca & forlet hine <foreign>Misit rex et soluit eum princeps populorum et dimisit eum</foreign>.
104.21. & he gesette hine drihtyn husys his & ealdormann eallre æhte his <foreign>Et constituit eum dominum domus sue et principem omnis possessionis sue</foreign>.
104.22. Þæt he gelærde ealdormenn his swa swa hyne sylfne & uðwiton his gleawnyss lærde <foreign>Vt erudiret principes suos sicut se ipsum et seniores suos prudentiam doceret</foreign>.
104.23. & inneode israhel on ægyptum & iacob eardode on eorðan chanaan <foreign>Et intrauit israhel in egyptum et iacob habitauit in terra chanaan</foreign>.
104.24. & geicte folc his swiðe & getrymyde hine ofyr fynd his <foreign>Et ausit populum suum nimis et confirmauit eum super inimicos eius</foreign>.
104.25. Gecyrryd heorte hyra þæt hi feodon folc his & facyn dydyn on þeowas his <foreign>Conuertit cor eorum ut odirent populum eius et dolum facerent in seruos eius</foreign>.
104.26. Sende moisen þeow his & aaron þone geceas hine <foreign>Misit moysen seruum suum et aaron quem elegit ipsum</foreign>.
104.27. Sette on him word tacna hyra & biecna hyra on eorðan chanaan <foreign>Posuit in eis uerba signorum suorum et prodigiorum suorum in terra chanaan</foreign>.
104.28. Sende þystru & aðystrode hie forþon ascunydon word his <foreign>Misit tenebras et obscurauit eos quia exacerbauerunt sermones eius</foreign>.
104.29. Gecyrde wætru hyra on blod & ofsloh fixas hyra <foreign>Conuertit aquas eorum in sanguinem et occidit pisces eorum</foreign>.
104.30. Sende on eorðan hyra froxas & on gebedclyfum cyninga hyra <foreign>Misit in terram eorum ranas et in cubilibus regum ipsorum</foreign>.
104.31. Cwæð & cwom hundes peo & gnætt on eallum endum hyra <foreign>Dixit et uenit cynomia et sciniphes in omnibus finibus eorum</foreign>.
104.32. Sette renas heora on hagul fyryne forbærnynde on eorðan hyra <foreign>Posuit pluuias eorum in grandinem ignem conburentem in terram ipsorum</foreign>.
104.33. & sloh wingeardas hyra & fictreow heora & forþræste ealle treow gemæra hyra <foreign>Et percussit uineas eorum et ficulneas eorum et contriuit omne lignum finium eorum</foreign>.
104.34. Cwæð & cwom gærshoppe & emel vel ceafyr þæs næs getel <foreign>Dixit et uenit locusta et bruchus cuius non erat numerus</foreign>.
104.35. & æt ealle heg eorðan hyra <foreign>et comedit omne fenum terre eorum</foreign>.
104.36. & sloh ælc frumbearn on eorðan egypta fruman ælcys geswincys hyra <foreign>Et percussit omne primogenitum in terra egypti primitias omnis laboris eorum</foreign>.
104.37. Utalædde hi on sylfure & golde & næs on cynryn hyra untrum <foreign>Et eduxit eos in argento et auro et non erat in tribubus eorum infirmus</foreign>.
104.38. Geblissod ys egyptaland on forðfromunge hyra forþon þe gefeoll ege hyra ofyr hi <foreign>Letata est egiptus in profectione eorum quia cecidit timor eorum super eos</foreign>.
104.39. Aþenyð wolcyn on gescyldnysse hyra & fyr þæt hit lyhte him þurh niht <foreign>Expandit nubem in protectionem eorum et ignem ut luceret eis per noctem</foreign>.
104.40. Bædun flæsc & com heom erschenn & hlaf heofonys gefylde hi <foreign>Petierunt carnes et uenit eis coturnix et pane celi saturauit eos</foreign>.
104.41. Toslat stan & fleowun wætyr & gewitun on drigum flodum <foreign>Disrupit petram et fluxerunt aque et abierunt in sicco flumina</foreign>.
104.42. Forþan gemyndig wæs wordys haligys his þæt sprecynde ys to abraham cniht his <foreign>Quia memor fuit uerbi sancti sui quod locutus est ad abraham puerum suum</foreign>.
104.43. & utalædde folc his on wynsumnysse & þa gecorenan his on blisse <foreign>Ed eduxit populum suum in exultatione et electos suos in letitia</foreign>.
104.44. & sealde him land þeoda & gewinn folca gesettun <foreign>Et dedit illis regiones gentium et labores populorum possiderunt</foreign>.
104.45. Þæt hi heold rihtwisnysse his & æ his secyn <foreign>Vt custodiant iustificationes eius et legem eius exquirant</foreign>.
105.1. Andyttað drihtne forþon god forþon on worulde mildheortnyss his <foreign>Confitemini domino quoniam bonus quoniam in seculum misericordia eius</foreign>.
105.2. Hwylc sprecð mihte drihtnys gehyrde gedo ealle lofu his <foreign>Quis loquetur potentias domini auditas faciet omnes laudes eius</foreign>.
105.3. Eadige þa þe healdað dom & dooð rihtwisnysse on ealle tid <foreign>Beati qui custodiunt iudicium et faciunt iustitias in omni tempore</foreign>.
105.4. Gemyne ure drihtyn on welgelicudvn folcys þinys neosa us on hæle þinre <foreign>Memento nostri domine in beneplacito populi tui uisita nos in salutari tuo</foreign>.
105.5. To geseonne on godnyssæ gecorynra þinra to blissiynne on blisse þeode þinre þæt þu sy heryd mid yrfeweardnysse þinre <foreign>Ad uidendum in bonitate electorum tuorum ad letandum in letitia gentis tue ut lauderis cum hereditate tua</foreign>.
105.6. We gesyngodon mid fædrum urum unrihtlice we dydon unrihtwisnysse we dydon <foreign>Peccauimus cum patribus nostris iniuste egimus iniquitatem fecimus</foreign>.
105.7. Fædras ure on egyptum ne ongetun wundyr þin & ne wæron gemyndige mænige mildheortnysse þinre & bysmrydon upstigynde on readan sæ <foreign>Patres nostri in egypto non intellexerunt mirabilia tua et non fuerunt memores multitudinis misericordie tue et inritauerunt ascendentes in rubrum mare</foreign>.
