134.19. Gehusscype israhela folcys bledsiað drihtyn gehusscype aaronys bledsiað drihtyn <foreign>Domus israhel benedicite dominum domus aaron benedicite dominum</foreign>.
134.20. Gehusscype lefiys bledsiað drihtyn þa þe ondrædað drihtyn bledsiað drihtyn <foreign>domus leui benedicite dominum qui timetis dominum benedicite dominum</foreign>.
134.21. Gebledsod drihtyn of sion se eardað on hierusalem <foreign>benedictus dominus ex sion qui habitað in hierusalem</foreign>.
135.1. Andyttað drihtne forþan god forþan on worulde mildheortnys his <foreign>confitemini domino quoniam bonus quoniam in seculum misericordia eius</foreign>.
135.2. Andyttað gode goda <foreign>Confitemini deo deorum quoniam</foreign>.
135.3. Andyttað drihtne drihtna <foreign>Confitemini domino dominorum quoniam</foreign>.
135.4. Se dyde wundur micyl ana <foreign>Qui fecit mirabilia magna solus quoniam</foreign>.
135.5. Se dyde hefynas on andgyte <foreign>Qui fecit celos in intellectu quoniam</foreign>.
135.6. Se gestaþolode eorðan ofyr wætru <foreign>Qui fundauit terram super aquas quoniam</foreign>.
135.7. Se dyde leohtfatu micle ana <foreign>Qui fecit luminaria magna solus quoniam</foreign>.
135.8. Sunnan on mihte dægys <foreign>Solem in potestatem diei quoniam</foreign>.
135.9. Monan & steorran on mihte nihtys <foreign>Lunam et stellas in potestatem noctis</foreign>.
135.10. Se sloh aegypte mid fruman heora <foreign>Qui percussit egyptum cum primitiis eorum</foreign>.
135.11. & utalædde of midle his <foreign>Et eduxit israhel de medio eius</foreign>.
135.12. On strang strangre & earme heaum <foreign>In manu forti et brachio excelso</foreign>.
135.13. Se todælde sæ reade on todælydnysse <foreign>Qui diuisit mare rubrum in diuisiones</foreign>.
135.14. & utalædde þurh midel his <foreign>Et eduxit israhel per medium eius</foreign>.
135.15. Aswegde & weryde his on sæ readre <foreign>Et excussit pharaonem et exercitum eius in mari rubro</foreign>.
135.16. Se alædde folc his þurh westyn <foreign>Qui transduxit populum suum per desertum</foreign>.
135.17. Se utalædde wætyr of stane clyfys se sloh cynyngas micle <foreign>Qui eduxit aquam de petra rupis qui percussit reges magnos</foreign>.
135.18. & he ofsloh cynyngas wundorlice <foreign>Et occidit reges mirabiles</foreign>.
135.19. Seon cyning amorrea <foreign>Seon regem amorreorum</foreign>.
135.20. & og cyning basan & ealle & ricu chanaanys he ofsloh <foreign>Et og regem basan et omnia regna chanaan occidit</foreign>.
135.21. & sealde eorðan hyra yrfeweardnysse <foreign>Et dedit terram eorum hereditatem</foreign>.
135.22. Yrfe israhelys þeowe his <foreign>hereditatem israhel seruo suo</foreign>.
135.23. Forþon on eadmodnysse ure gemyndig wæs ure drihtyn <foreign>Quia in humilitate nostra memor fuit nostri dominus</foreign>.
135.24. & he alysyð us of handa feonda ure <foreign>Et redemit nos de manu inimicorum nostrorum</foreign>.
135.25. Se sylyð mete ælcum flæsce <foreign>Qui dat escam omni carni</foreign>.
135.26. Andyttað gode hefynys andyttað drihtne drihtna forþon god forþon on worulde mildheortnys his <foreign>Confitemini deo celi confitemini domino dominorum quoniam bonus quoniam in seculum misericordia eius</foreign>.
136.1. Ofyr flodas babilonys þær we sætvn & weopun þa þa we wæron gemyndige þinys sion <foreign>Svper flvmina babilonis illic sedimus et fleuimus dum recordaremur tui sion</foreign>.
136.2. On sealum on midle his we hengon organan ure <foreign>In sallicibus in medio eius suspendimus organa nostra</foreign>.
136.3. Forþon þær frunum vel ahsodon us þa gehæfte gelæddon us word songa & þa þe wiðlæddon us ymyn singað us of sangum sion <foreign>Quia illis interrogauerunt nos qui captiuos duxerunt nos uerba cantionum et qui abduxerunt nos hymnum cantate nobis de canticis sion</foreign>.
136.4. Hu singað we sang drihtnys on eorðan fremdre <foreign>quomodo cantabimus canticum domini in terra aliena</foreign>.
136.5. Gef ofyrgytyn ic beom þin hierusalem ofyrgytyð me seo swiðre min <foreign>Si oblitus fuero tui hierusalem obliuiscatur me dextera mea</foreign>.
136.6. Ætfeolyð vel genealæce tunge min gomum minum gif ne gemyne þin gef ic ne foresette hierusalem on fruman blisse mine <foreign>adhereat lingua mea faucimus meis si non meminero tui si non proposuero hierusalem in principio letitie mee</foreign>.
136.7. Gemun þu drihtyn bearna edomys on dæge hierusalem þa cweðað aidliað aidliað hu lange oð staðul on hyre <foreign>Memento domine filiorum edom in die hierusalem qui dicunt exinanite exinanite quousque ad fundamentum in ea</foreign>.
136.8. Dohtor babilonys earmre eadig se geedleanað þe edlean þæt þu þu geedleanodyst us <foreign>Filia babilonis misera beatus qui retribuit tibi retributionem quam tu retribuisti nobis</foreign>.
136.9. Eadig se þe nimyð & gecnysyð þa lytlan his to stane <foreign>Beatus qui tenebit et allidet paruulos suos ad petram</foreign>.
137.1. Ic andytte þe drihtyn on ealre heortan minre forþon þu gehyrdyst ealle word muðys minys & on gesihðe engla ic singe þe <foreign>Confitebor tibi domine in toto corde meo quoniam exaudisti omnia uerba oris mei et in conspectu angelorum psallam tibi</foreign>.
137.2. Ic wurðie & gebidde to temple þam halgan þinum & ic andytte naman þinum ofyr mildheortnysse þine & soðfæstnysse þine forþon gemiclodyst ofyr us naman halgan þinne <foreign>Adorabo ad templum sanctum tuum et confitebor nomini tuo super misericordia tua et ueritate tua quoniam magnificasti super nos nomen sanctum tuum</foreign>.
137.3. On swa hwylcum dæge ic gecige þe gehyr me þu gemænigfealdodyst on sawle mine mægn þin <foreign>In quacumque die inuocauero te exaudi me multiplicabis in anima mea uirtutem tuam</foreign>.
137.4. Andyttyn þe drihtyn ealle cyningas eorðan forþon gehyrdon ealle word muðys þinys <foreign>Confiteantur tibi domine omnes reges terre quoniam audierunt omnia uerba oris tui</foreign>.
137.5. & singyn on sangum drihtyn forþon micyl ys wuldur drihtnys <foreign>et cantent in canticis domino quoniam magna est gloria domini</foreign>.
137.6. Forþon se hea drihtyn & þa eaðmodan he gelocað & þa hean feorran he oncnæwyð <foreign>quoniam excelsus dominus et humilia respicit et alta a longe agnoscit</foreign>.
137.7. Þehþe ic gange on midle geswincys þu geliffæstyst me & ofyr yrre feonda minra þu aþenydyst hand þin & halne me dyde swiðre þin <foreign>Si ambulauero in medio tribulationis uiuificabis me et super iram inimicorum meorum extendisti manum tuam et saluum me fecit dextera tua</foreign>.
137.8. Drihtyn agyld for me drihtyn mildheortnys þin on worulde & worc handa þinra ne forseoh ðu <foreign>Domine retribue pro me domine misericordia tua in seculum et opera manuum tuarum ne despicias</foreign>.
138.1. Drihtyn þu cunnudyst me & þu oncnewe me <foreign>Domine probasti me et cognouisti me</foreign>.
138.2. Þu oncnewe gesetynesse mine & æryste mine <foreign>tu cognouisti sessionem meam et resurrectionem meam</foreign>.
138.3. Þu ongete geþohtas mine feorran stige mine & gerecynysse mine þu aspyrydyst <foreign>Intellexisti cogitationes meas a longe semitam meam et directionem meam inuestigasti</foreign>.
138.4. & ealle wegas mine þu foresceawod forþon nys facyn on tungan minre <foreign>et omnes uias meas preuidisti quia non est dolus in lingua mea</foreign>.
138.5. Efne þu drihtyn gecnewe ealle niwe & þa ealdan þu gehyrdyst me & þu gesettyst ofyr me hand þine <foreign>Ecce tu domine cognouisti omnia nouissima et antiqua tu formasti me et posuisti super me manum tuam</foreign>.
138.6. Wundurlic gewordyn ys wisdom þin of me gestrangod ys ne ic ne mæg to him <foreign>Mirabilis facta est scientia tua ex me confortata est nec potero ad eum</foreign>.
138.7. Hwidyr gange ic fram gaste þinum & fram ansyne þinre hwidyr ic fleo <foreign>Quo ibo spiritu tuo et a facie tua quo fugiam</foreign>.
138.8. Gif ic astige on hefun þu þær eart gif ic aduneastige on helle æt eart þu <foreign>Si ascendero in celum tu illic es si descendero in infernum ades</foreign>.
138.9. Gif ic nyme fiðru mine ær leohte & ic eardige on þam utymystan sæ <foreign>Si sumsero pennas meas ante lucem et habitauero in postremo maris</foreign>.
138.10. & soðlice þær hand þin gelædyð me & nymyð me swiðre þin <foreign>Etenim illuc manus tua deducet me et tenebit me dextera tua</foreign>.
138.11. & ic cwæð weninga þystru betredað me & niht onlyhtydnys min on wistum minum <foreign>Et dixi forsitan tenebre conculcabunt me et nox inluminatio mea in deliciis meis</foreign>.
138.12. Forþon þyrtre ne beoð aðystrude fram þe & niht swa swa dæg bið onlihtyd swa swa þystru his swa & leoht his <foreign>Quia tenebre non obscurabuntur abs te et nox sicut dies inluminabitur sicut tenebre eius ita et lumen eius</foreign>.
138.13. Forþon þu drihtyn gesettyst æddran mine onfenge me of innoðe modur minre <foreign>quia tu domine possedisti renes meos suscepisti me de utero matris meae</foreign>.
138.14. Ic andytte þe drihtyn forþon egysfullice gewundrud eart wundur worc þin & sawl min wat swiðe <foreign>Confitebor tibi domine quoniam terribiliter mirificatus es mira opera tua et anima mea nouit nimis</foreign>.
138.15. Nys gediglod muð min fram þe þæt þu dydyst on digylnysse & speda mina on þam nyðyrrum eorðan <foreign>Non est occultatum os meum abs te quod fecisti in occulto et substantia mea in inferioribus terre</foreign>.
138.16. On fullfremydnysse mine gesawon eagan þine & on bec þinre ealle syn awrityne dagas beoð getrymyde & nænig ne on him <foreign>Inperfectum meum uiderunt oculi tui et in libro tuo omnes scribentur die formabuntur et nemo in eis</foreign>.
138.17. Me soðlice swiðe gearode wurðude me synd frynd þine god swiðe gestrangod ys ealdordomas hyra <foreign>mihi autem nimis honorificati sunt amici tui deus nimis confortatus est principatus eorum</foreign>.
138.18. Ic atelle hi & ofyr sand cysel beoð gemænigfealdode ic aras & nugyt myd þe ic eom <foreign>Dinumerabo eos et super arenam multiplicabuntur resurrexi et adhuc tecum sum</foreign>.
138.19. Gif þu ofslyhst god synfulle weras bloda onhyldað fram me <foreign>si occideris deus peccatores viri sanguinum declinatæ a me</foreign>.
138.20. Forþan ge cweðað secgað on geþohtum urum onfon hi on idylnysse cestre his <foreign>quia dicitis in cogitationibus uestris accipiant in uanite ciuitates suas</foreign>.
138.21. Hune þa þe þe feodun hatedon god ic feode ic hatedon/ þa & ofyr fynd þine ic aswand <foreign>Nonne qui te oderunt deus oderam illos et super inimicos tuos tabescebam</foreign>.
138.22. Fullfremydre hatunge ic feode ic hatedon hi fynd gewordyne synd me <foreign>Perfecto odio oderam illos inimici facti sunt mihi</foreign>.
138.23. Fanda min god & wite þu heortan mine ahsa me & gecnæw stige siþfate mine <foreign>Proba me deus et scito cor meum interroga me et cognosce semitas meas</foreign>.
138.24. & geseoh gef hwæðere unrihtwisnysse on me ys & gelæd me on weg ecne <foreign>Et uide si uia iniquitatis in me est et deduc me in uia eterna</foreign>.
139.2. Genere me drihtyn fram men yflum fram were unrihtwisum alys me <foreign>Eripe me domine ab homine malo a uiro iniquo libera me</foreign>.
139.3. Þa þohton hætas on heortan ealne dæg gesettvn gefeoht <foreign>Qui cogitauerunt malitias in corde tota die constituebant proelia</foreign>.
139.4. Scyrptun tungan hyra swa swa nædran attor nædryna undyr welyrum hyra <foreign>Acuerunt linguas suas sicut serpentes uenenum aspidum sub labiis eorum</foreign>.
139.5. Heald me drihtyn of handa synfullys fram mannum unrihtwisum gefreo me þa þohton gescrencean gangas mine <foreign>Custodi me domine de manu peccatoris ab hominibus iniquis libera me qui cogitauerunt subplantare gressus meos</foreign>.
139.6. Ahyddon ofyrhogan gryne me & rapas aþenydon on gryne fotum minum wið wege æswic gesetton me <foreign>absconderunt superbi laqueos mihi et funes extenderunt in laqueo pedibus meis iuxta iter scandalum poserunt mihi</foreign>.
139.7. Ic cwæð to drihtne god min eart þu gehyr drihtyn stefne gebedys minys <foreign>Dixi domino deus meus es tu exaudi domine uocem orationis mee</foreign>.
139.8. Drihtyn drihtyn mægyn hælo minre ofyrsceada heafod min on dæge gefeohtys <foreign>Domine domine uirtus salutis mee obumbra caput meum in die belli</foreign>.
139.9. Ne gesyle me luste minum synnfulle þohton ongen me ne forlæt þu me þelæs æfre syn uppahafyne <foreign>Ne tradas me a desiderio meo peccatores cogitauerunt aduersum me ne derelinquas me ne umquam exaltentur</foreign>.
139.10. Heafod ymbhwyrftys hyra gewinn welyra hyra ofyrwryhð hi <foreign>Caput circuitus eorum labor labiorum ipsorum operiet eos</foreign>.
139.11. Feallað ofyr hi colu fyrys on fyre þu aworpyst hi on yrmþum ne wiðstandað <foreign>Cadent super eos carbones ignis in ignem deiecies eos in miseriis non subsistent</foreign>.
139.12. Wer getinge ne bið gereht ofyr eorðan wer þone unrihtan yfyl hi nymað on forwyrde <foreign>Vir linguosus non dirietur super terram uirum iniustum mala capient in interitum</foreign>.
139.13. Ic oncnew forþon deð drihtyn dom wædlyna & wrace þearfyna <foreign>Cognoui quoniam faciet dominus iudicium inopum et uindictam pauperum</foreign>.
139.14. Þehhwæðere rihtwise andyttað naman þinum & eardiað rihtwise mid andwlitan þinum <foreign>Uerumtamen iusti confitebuntur nomini tuo et habitabunt recti cum uultu tuo</foreign>.
140.1. Drihtyn ic clypode to þe gehyr me beheald stefne gebedys minys þonne ic clypige to þe <foreign>Domine clamavi ad te exaudi me intende uoci orationis mee dum clauero ad te</foreign>.
140.2. Syn gereht gebed min swa swa ricylsum vel stor on gesihðe þine gesihðe upahafennys handa minra onsægdnys æfynlice <foreign>Dirigatur oratio mea sicut incensum in conspectu tuo eleuatio manuum mearum sacrificium uespertinum</foreign>.
140.3. Sete drihtyn gehyd muðe minum & duru ymbstandydnysse welerum minum <foreign>Pone domine custodiam ori meo et ostium circumstantie labiis meis</foreign>.
140.4. Þæt þu ne onhylde heortan mine on word yfyl to oncunnyne oncunnysse on synnum mid mannum wyrcyndum unrihtwisnysse & ic ne gelæce mæsumige mid gecorenum hyra <foreign>Vt non declines cor meum in uerbum malum ad excussandas excussationes in peccatis cum hominibus operantibus iniquitatem et non comminabor cum electis eorum</foreign>.
140.5. Þreað me rihtwis on mildheortnysse & þreað me ele soðlice synfullys ne smyryð bedypiþ heafod min forþon nugyt ys gebed min on welgelicodum hyra <foreign>Corripiet me iustus in misericordia et increpauit me oleum autem peccatoris non inpinguet caput meum quoniam adhuc est oratio mea in beneplacitis eorum</foreign>.
140.6. Forswolgyne synd wið stane deman hyra gehyryn word min forþon mihton <foreign>absorti sunt iuxta petram iudices eorum audient uerba mea quoniam potuerunt</foreign>.
140.7. Swa swa fætnys eorðan wæs tosliten ofyr eorðan tostencyde synd ban ure nieh helle <foreign>Sicut crassitudo terre eructuat super terram dissipata sunt ossa nostra secus infernum</foreign>.
140.8. Forþon to ðe drihtyn drihtyn eagan mine on þe ic gehihte ne afyr þu sawle mine <foreign>Quia ad te domine domine oculi mei in te speraui ne auferas animam meam</foreign>.
140.9. Geheald me fram gryne þa gesettun me & fram æswicum wyrcyndum urrihtwisnysse <foreign>Custodi me a laqueo quem statuerunt mihi et ab scandalis operantium iniquitatem</foreign>.
140.10. Feallað on nette his synfulle syndyrlice eom ic oðþæt ic geleore fare <foreign>Cadent in rectiacula eius peccatores singulariter sum ego donec transeam</foreign>.
141.2. Myd stefne minre to drihtne ic clypige myd stefne minre to gode biddynde ic eom <foreign>Voce mea ad dominvm clamaui uoce mea ad deum deprecatus sum</foreign>.
141.3. Ic ageote on gesihðe his gebed min & geswencydnysse mine beforan him ic forðsecge <foreign>Effundam in conspectu eius orationem meam et tribulationem meam ante ipsum pronuntio</foreign>.
141.4. On ateorunge on me gast minne & þu oncnewe stige mine on wege þissum on þam ic ymbgange ahyddon grynu me <foreign>In deficiendo in me spiritum meum et tu cognouisti semitas meas in uia hac qua ambulabam absconderunt superbi laqueos mihi</foreign>.
141.5. Ic sceawode to þære swiðran & i geseah & næs þe oncnewe me forwearð fleam fram me & nys se sece sawle mine <foreign>considerabam ad dexteram et uidebam et non erat qui agnosceret me periit fuga a me et non est qui requirat animam meam</foreign>.
141.6. Ic clypode to þe drihtyn ic cwæð þu eart hiht min dæl min on eorðan lyfygyndra <foreign>clamaui ad te domine dixi tu es spes mea portio mea in terra uiuentium</foreign>.
141.7. Beheald on gebede min forðon geeadmodud ic eom swiðe alys me fram þam ehtyndum me forþon gestrangode sund ofyr me <foreign>Intende in orationem meam quia humiliatus sum nimis libera me a persequentibus me quoniam confortati sunt super me</foreign>.
141.8. Gelæd of carcerne sawl mine to andyttynne naman þinum me gebiddað rihtwise oðþæt þu geleanige me <foreign>Educ de carcere animam meam ad confitendum nomini tuo me expectant iusti donec retribuas mihi</foreign>.
142.1. Drihtyn gehyr gebed min mid earum onfoh hælsunge mine on soðfæstnysse þinre gehyr me on þinre rihtwisnysse <foreign>Domine exavdi orationem meam auribus percipe obsecrationem meam in ueritate tua exaudi me in tua iustitia</foreign>.
142.2. & ne ga þu inn on dome mid þeowe þinum forþon ne bið gerihtwisod on gesihðe þinre ælc lybbynde <foreign>Et non intres in iudicium cum seruo tuo quia non iustificabitur in conspectu tuo omnis uiuens</foreign>.
142.3. Forþon iehtynde ys fynd sawle mine geeaðmodode on eorþan lif min gestaðolode me on digulnysse swa swa deade worulde <foreign>Quia persecutus est inimicus animam meam humiliauit in terra uitam meam collocauit me in obscuris sicut mortuus seculi</foreign>.
142.4. & genyrwyd ys on me gast min on me gedrefyd ys heorte min <foreign>et anxiatus est in me spiritus meus in me turbatum est cor meum</foreign>.
142.5. Gemyndig ic wæs daga ealdra & smeagynde ic eom on eallum worcum þinum & on dædum handa þinra ic smeage <foreign>Memor fui dierum antiquorum et meditatus sum in omnibus operibus tuis et in factis manuum tuarum meditabor</foreign>.
142.6. Ic þenyde handa mine to þe sawl min swa swa eorðe butan wætyre þe <foreign>Expandi manus meas ad te anima mea sicut terra sine aqua tibi</foreign>.
142.7. Hrædlice gehyr me drihtyn ateorude gast min ne afyr þu onsyne þin fram me & ic beom gelic astigyndum on seað <foreign>uelociter exaudi me domine defecit spiritus meus ne auertas faciem tuam a me et ero similis descendentibus in lacum</foreign>.
142.8. Geherde me doa on morgynne mildheortnysse þine forþon on þe ic gehihte drihtyn cuðne me doa weg on þam ic gange forþon to þe drihtyn ic uppahof sawle mine <foreign>Auditam mihi fac mane misericordiam tuam quia in te speraui domine notam mihi fac uiam in qua ambulem quia ad te domine leuaui animam meam</foreign>.
142.9. Genere me of feondum minum drihtyn to þe ic flieh <foreign>Eripe me de inimicis meis domine ad te confugi</foreign>.
142.10. Lær me don willan þin forþan þu eart god min gast þin god gelædyð me on weg rihtne <foreign>doce me facere uoluntatem tuam quia tu est deus meus spiritus tuus bonus deducet me in uia recta</foreign>.
142.11. Fore naman þinum drihtyn þu geliffæstyst me on rihtwisnysse/ þinre & utalædyst of geswince sawle mine <foreign>propter nomen tuum domine uiuificabis me in equitate tua et educes de tribulatione animam meam</foreign>.
142.12. & on mildehortnysse þine þu tostencst fynd mine & þu forspildyst ealle þa þe swenceað sawle mine forþon þeow þin ic eom <foreign>et in misericordia tua disperdes inimicos meos et perdes omnes qui tribulant animam meam quoniam seruus tuus ego sum</foreign>.
143.1. Gebledsod drihtyn god min se lærð hand mine to gefeohte & fingras mine to campe <foreign>Benedictvs dominus deus meus qui docet manus meas ad prelium et digitos meos ad bellum</foreign>.
143.2. Mildheortnys min & gebeorh min andfenga min & alyssynd min gescyldynd min & on him ic gehihte undyrþeodynde folc undyr me <foreign>Misericordia mea et refugium meum susceptor meus et liberator meus protector meus et in ipso speraui subiciens populos sub me</foreign>.
143.3. Drihtyn hwæt ys mann þæt þu cuðudyst him oððe bearn manna forþon getelyst hine <foreign>Domine quid est homo quid innotuisti ei aut filius hominis quoniam reputas eum</foreign>.
143.4. Mann idylnysse gelic gewordyn ys dæg his swa swa sceadu forðgeleorað <foreign>Homo uanitatis similis factus est dies eius sicut umbra pretereunt</foreign>.
143.5. Drihtyn onhyld hefonas þine & niðyrastihð æthrin muntas & hi smeocað <foreign>Domine inclina celos tuos et discende tange montes et fumigabunt</foreign>.
143.6. Bliccytte bliccytvnge þine & þu tostencyst hi onsend flana þine & þu gedrefst hi <foreign>Corusca coruscationes tuae et dissipabis eos emitte sagittas tuas et conturbabis eos</foreign>.
143.7. Onsend hand þine of heanysse genere me & alys me of wætrum miclum & of handa bearna fremdra <foreign>Emitte manum tuam de alto eripe me et libera me de aquis multis et de manu filiorum alienorum</foreign>.
143.8. Þara muð sprecynde ys idylnysse & seo swiþere hyra swiðere unrihtwisnysse <foreign>Quorum os locutum est uanitatem et dextera eorum dextera iniquitatis</foreign>.
143.9. God sang niwne ic singe þe on hearpan on saltere tyn strenge ic singe þe <foreign>Deus canticum nouum cantabo tibi in psalterio decem chordarum psallam tibi</foreign>.
143.10. Þu sylyst hæle cynyngum þu gefreost dauid þeow þinne of swurde awyrgyde <foreign>Qui das salutem regibus qui liberasti dauid seruum tuum de gladio maligno</foreign>.
143.11. Genere me & gefreo me of wætrum miclum & of handa bearna fremdra þara muð sprecynde wæs idylnysse & seo swiðre hyra swiðre unrihtwisnysse <foreign>Eripe me et libera me de aquis multis et de manu filiorum alienorum quorum os locutum est uanitatem et dextera eorum dextera iniquitatis</foreign>.
143.12. Þara bearn swa swa niwe plantunge gestaðolfæstod fram iuguþe his dohtra hyra geglengyd geset ymbgefrætwude swa swa gelicnys templys <foreign>Quorum filii sicut nouelle plantationis stabiliti a iuuentute sua filii eorum conposite circumornate ut similitudo templi</foreign>.
143.13. Hordyrn vel wyrtgeardas hyra full recetunge of þyssum on þæt scep hyra berynde melce genihtsumiynde on siðfætum hyra <foreign>Prumptuaria eorum plena eructuantia ex hoc in illud oues eorum fetose abundantes in itineribus suis</foreign>.
143.14. Oxan heora fætte nys hryre stanwealles ne forlætnys ne clypung on strætum hyra <foreign>boues eorum crassi non est ruina macerie neque transitus neque clamor in plateis eorum</foreign>.
143.15. Eadig cwædun folc þam þæs synd eadig folc þæs ys drihtyn god hyra <foreign>Beatum dixerunt populum cui hec sunt beatus populus cuius est dominus deus eorum</foreign>.
144.1. Ic upahebbe þe god cyning min & bledsie naman þinne on ecnysse & on woruld worulde <foreign>Exaltabo te deus rex meus et benedicam nomen tuum in eternum et in seculum seculi</foreign>.
144.2. Þurh syngale dagas ic bledsie þe & ic herie naman þinne on ecnysse & on woruld worulde <foreign>Per singulos dies benedicam te et laudabo nomen tuum in eternum et in seculum seculi</foreign>.
144.3. Micyl drihtyn & hergyndlic swiðe & mycylnysse his nys ende <foreign>Magnus dominus et laudabilis nimis et magnitudinis eius non est finis</foreign>.
144.4. Cneoriss & cneoryss hergað worc þin & mihte þine forðsecgað <foreign>Generatio et generatio laudabunt opera tua et potentiam tuam pronuntiabunt</foreign>.
144.5. Micylnysse mægynþrymmys þine & halignysse þine sprecað & wundur þin secgað <foreign>Magnificentiam maiestatis tue et sanctitatem tuam loquentur et mirabilia tua narrabunt</foreign>.
144.6. Mægyn egysfullice þinra cweðað & micylnysse þine secgað <foreign>Virtutem terribiliorum tuorum dicent et magnitudinem tuam narrabunt</foreign>.
144.7. Gemynd genihtsumnysse wynsumnysse þinre roccytað & rihtwisnysse þine gefeoð <foreign>Memoriam abundantie suauitatis tue eructabunt et iustitiam tuam exultabunt</foreign>.
144.8. Mildheort & myltsiynd drihtyn geþyldig & swiðe mildheort <foreign>Misericors et miserator dominus patiens et multum misericors</foreign>.
144.9. Wynsum drihtyn eallum & myldse his ofyr ealle worc his <foreign>Suauis dominus uniuersis et miserationes eius super omnia opera eius</foreign>.
144.10. Andyttað þe drihtyn ealle worc þine & halige þine bledsiað þe <foreign>Confiteantur tibi domine omnia opera tua et sancti tui benedicent te</foreign>.
144.11. Wuldur ricys þinys cweðað & mihta þine sprecað <foreign>Gloriam regni tui dicent et potentiam tuam loquentur</foreign>.
144.12. Þæt cuðe don bearnum manna mihte þine & wuldur micylnysse ricys þinys <foreign>Ut notam faciant filiis hominum potentiam tuam et gloriam magnificentie regni tui</foreign>.
144.13. Rice þine drihtyn rice ealra worulda & wealnyss þin on ealre cneorisse & cynne getrywe drihtyn on wordum his & halig on eallum worcum hys <foreign>Regnum tuum domine regnum omnium seculorum et dominatio tua in omni generatione et progenie fidelis dominus in uerbis suis et sanctus in omnibus operibus suis</foreign>.
144.14. Uppahefð drihtyn ealle þa þe feallað vel hreosað & gerecyð ealle gecnysyde <foreign>Alleuat dominus omnes qui ruunt et erigit omnes elisos</foreign>.
144.15. Eagan eallra on þe gehihtað drihtyn & þu sylyst mete him on tide gelimplicre oððe gedefre <foreign>Oculi omnium in te sperant domine et tu das escam illis in tempore oportuno</foreign>.
144.16. Ontynyst þu hand þine & gefyllyst ælc neat vel wiht bledsunge <foreign>Aperis tu manum tuam et imples omne animal benedictione</foreign>.
144.17. Rihtwis drihtyn on eallum wegas his & halig on eallum worcum his <foreign>Iustus dominus in omnibus uiis suis et sanctus in omnibus operibus suis</foreign>.
144.18. Nieh ys drihtyn eallum gecigyndum hine on soðfæstnysse <foreign>Prope est dominus omnibus inuocantibus eum in ueritate</foreign>.
144.19. Willan ondrædyndra hine deð gebedu hyra gehyryð & hale gedeð hi <foreign>Uoluntatem timentium se faciet orationes eorum exaudiet et saluos faciet eos</foreign>.
144.20. Healdyð drihtyn ealle lufiynde hine & ealle synfulle tostencyð <foreign>Custodit dominus omnes diligentes se et omnes peccatores disperdit</foreign>.
144.21. Lof drihtnys sprecyð muð min & bledsie ælc flæsc naman halgan his on ecnysse et on woruld worulde <foreign>Laudem domini loquetur os meum et benedicat omnis caro nomen sanctum eius in eternum et in seculum seculi</foreign>.
145.2. Here sawle mine here drihtyn ic herge drihtyn on life minum ic singe gode minum swa lange swa ic beom nellað ge getrywan on ealdormannum <foreign>Lavda anima mea dominum ladabo dominum in uita mea psallam deo meo quamdiu ero nolite confidere in principibus</foreign>.
145.3. Ne on bearnum manna on þam nys hæle <foreign>neque in filiis hominum in quibus non est salus</foreign>.
145.4. Utgæð gast his & eftcyrryð on eorðan his on þam dæge forwurðaþ ealle geþohtas hyra <foreign>Exiet spiritus eius et reuertetur in terram suam in illa die peribunt omnes cogitationes eorum</foreign>.
145.5. Eadig þæs god iacobys fultum his & hiht his on drihtne gode his <foreign>Beatus cuius deus iacob adiutor eius et spes eius in domino deo ipsius</foreign>.
145.6. Se worhte hefun & eorðan sæ & ealle þe on þam synd <foreign>Qui fecit celum et terram mare et omnia que in eis sunt</foreign>.
145.7. Se healdyð soðfæstnysse on worulde deð dom teonan geþyldigum sylyð mete hingriyndum drihtyn gerecyð gecnysyde drihtyn lysyð gecypsyde <foreign>Qui custodit ueritatem in seculum facit iudicium iniuriam patientibus dat escam esurientibus dominus erigit elisos dominus soluit conpeditos</foreign>.
145.8. Drihtyn onlyhtyð blinde drihtyn gerecð rihtwise <foreign>dominus inluminat cecos dominus dirigit iustos</foreign>.
145.9. Drihtyn healdyð wræccan fædyrleasne & wuduwan onfehð & weg synfulra tobrytyð <foreign>Dominus custodit aduenam pupillum et uiduam suscipiet et uiam peccatorum exterminabit</foreign>.
145.10. Ricsað drihtyn on ecnysse god þin sion on woruld worulde <foreign>Regnabit dominus in eternum deus tuus sion in seculum seculi</foreign>.
146.1. Hergað drihtyn forþon god ys salm gode urum wynsum sy herenes <foreign>Lavdate dominvm quoniam bonus est psalmus deo nostro iucunda sit</foreign>.
146.2. Timbriynde on heofonlicre sybgesyhðe drihtyn & tostencnysse israhelys gesamniynde <foreign>Aedificans hierusalem dominus et dispersiones israhel congregans</foreign>.
146.3. Se hælð geþræste heortan & onwriðyð forþræstydnysse heora <foreign>Qui sanat contritos corde et alligat contritiones eorum</foreign>.
146.4. Se rimyð mænigeo steorryna & eallum his naman cigð <foreign>Qui numerat multitudinem stellarum et omnibus eius nomina uocans</foreign>.
146.5. Micyl drihtyn ure & mycyl mægn his & snyttro his nys gerim <foreign>Magnus dominus noster et magna uirtus eius et sapientie eius non est numerus</foreign>.
146.6. Onfoynde manþwære drihtyn geeadmodað soðlice synfulle oð eorðan <foreign>Suscipiens mansuetos dominus humiliat autem peccatores usque ad terram</foreign>.
146.7. Ongynnað drihtne on andytnysse singað gode urum on cytran <foreign>Incipite domino in confesione psallite deo nostro in cythara</foreign>.
146.8. Se ofyrwrihð hefyn mid wolcnum & gearwað eorþan ren se forðlædyð on muntum heg & wyrta þeowdomys manna <foreign>Qui operit celum nubibus et parat terre pluuiam qui producit in montibus fenum et herbam seruituti hominum</foreign>.
146.9. Se sylyð neatum mete hyra & briddum hrefn gecigyndum hine <foreign>Qui dat iumentis escam ipsorum et pullis coruorum inuocantibus eum</foreign>.
146.10. Na on mægynum horsys willan hafað ne on geteldum werys wellicwurðe ys him <foreign>Non in uiribus equi uoluntatem habebit neque in tabernaculis uiri beneplacitum est ei</foreign>.
146.11. Welgelicod ys drihtne ofyr ondrædynde hine & on him þa gehihtað on mildheortnysse his <foreign>Beneplacitum est domino super timentes eum et in eos qui sperant in misericordia eius</foreign>.
147.1. Here hierusalem drihtyn here god þinne syon <foreign>Lavda hiervsalem dominum lauda deum tuum sion</foreign>.
147.2. Forþon gestrangode scyttyls gata þinra bledsode bearn þine on þe <foreign>Quoniam confortauit seras portarum tuarum benedixit filiis tuis in te</foreign>.
147.3. Se sette endas þine sible & smeru hwætys gefyllynde þe <foreign>Qui posuit fines tuos pacem et adipe frumenti satians te</foreign>.
147.4. Se utsendyð gesprec his eorþan hræddlice yrnyð word his <foreign>Qui emittit eloquium suum terre uelociter currit sermo eius</foreign>.
147.5. Se sylyð snaw swa swa wulla gesworc genip swa swa ahsan stregdyð <foreign>Qui dat niuem sicut lanam nebulam sicut cinerem aspergit</foreign>.
147.6. Sendyð gymm vel stan his swa swa sticce vel croman hlafys beforan ansyne cylys his hwylc wiðstandyð <foreign>Mittit christallum suum sicut frustam panis ante faciem frigoris eius qui subsistit</foreign>.
147.7. Sendyð word his & myltyð he deð þa bleow gast his & flowun wætyr <foreign>Mittit uerbum suum et liquefaciet ea flauit spiritus eius et fluent aque</foreign>.
147.8. Forðsecgynde word his iacob rihtwisnyssa & domas his israhel <foreign>Pronuntians uebum suum iacob iustias et iudicia sua israhel</foreign>.
147.9. Ne dyde swa ælcre cneorysse & domas his na geswutolode his <foreign>Non fecit taliter omni nationi et iudicia sua non manifestauit eis</foreign>.
148.1. Hergeað drihtyn of hefynum hergeað hine on heannysse <foreign>Lavdate dominvm de celis laudate eum in excelsis</foreign>.
148.2. Hergeað hine ealle englas his hergeað hine ealle mægynu his <foreign>Laudate eum omnes angeli eius laudate eum omnes uirtutes eius</foreign>.
148.3. Hergeað hine sunne & mona hergeað hine ealle steorran & leoht <foreign>Laudate eum sol et luna laudate eum omnes stelle et lumen</foreign>.
148.4. Hergeað hine hefnas hefyna & wætyr þa ofyr hefynas synd <foreign>Laudate eum celi celorum et aque que super celos sunt</foreign>.
148.5. Hergyn naman drihtnys forþon he cwæð & gewordyne synd he bebead & gesceapyne synd <foreign>laudent nomen domini quia ipse dixit et facta sunt ipse mandauit et creata sunt</foreign>.
148.6. Gesette þa on ecnysse & on woruld worulde bybod gesette & na beleorde forðeode <foreign>statuit ea in eternum et in seculum seculi preceptum posuit et non preteribit</foreign>.
148.7. Hergeað drihtyn of eorðan dracan & ealle nywilnysse <foreign>Laudate dominum de terra dracones et omnes abissi</foreign>.
148.8. Fyr hagol snaw is gast vel blæd ysta þa doð word his <foreign>Ignis grando nix glacies spiritus procellarum qui faciunt uerbum eius</foreign>.
148.9. Muntas & ealle hyllas treow wæstmbære & ealle cedyrbeam <foreign>Montes et omnes colles ligna fructifera et omnes cedri</foreign>.
148.10. Wildeor & ealle nytynu næddran & fuglas gefyðryde <foreign>Bestie et uniuersa pecora serpentes et uolucres pennate</foreign>.
148.11. Cyningas eorðan & ealle folcys ealdor & ealle deman eorðan <foreign>Reges terre et omnes populi principes et omnes iudices terre</foreign>.
148.12. Iunge & fæmnan ealde mid iungum hergeað naman drihtnys <foreign>Iuuenes et uirgines seniores cum iunioribus laudent nomen domini</foreign>.
148.13. Forþon uppahafyn is nama his anys <foreign>Quia exaltatum est nomen eius solius</foreign>.
148.14. Andyttnys his ofyr hefyn & eorðan & upahefð horn folcys his ymyn eallum halgum his bearnum israhela folce tonealæcyndum him <foreign>confessio eius super celum et terram et exaltauit cornu populi sui hymnum omnibus sanctis eius filiis israhel populo adpropianti sibi</foreign>.
149.1. Singað drihtne sang niwne herynys his on cyrcean haligra <foreign>Cantate domino canticvm nouum laudatio eius in ecclesia sanctorum</foreign>.
149.2. Blissie israhel on hire se deð hyne & dohtra sionys gefeon ofyr cyning his <foreign>Letetur israhel in eo qui fecit ipsum et filie sion exultent super regem suum</foreign>.
149.3. Hergeað naman his mid þreate on tympan & hearpan singað þe <foreign>Laudent nomen eius in choro in tymphano et psalterio psallant tibi</foreign>.
149.4. Forþon welgelicod ys drihtne on folce his & uppahebbað manþwærer on hæle <foreign>Quia beneplacitum est domino in populo suo et exaltauit mansuetos in salutem</foreign>.
149.5. Gefeoð halige on wuldre blissiað on bedclyfum his <foreign>Exaltabunt sancti in gloria letabuntur in cubilibus suis</foreign>.
149.6. Wynsumnysse godys on gomum hyra & swyrd twyecge on handum hyra <foreign>Exultationes dei in faucibus eorum et gladii ancipites in manibus eorum</foreign>.
149.7. To doynne wrace on cneoryssum þreaung on folce <foreign>Ad faciendam uindictam in nationibus increpationes in populis</foreign>.
149.8. To bindannæ cyningas hyra on fotcospum & æðyle hyra on bendum isynum <foreign>Ad alligandos reges eorum in conpedibus et nobiles eorum in uinculis ferreis</foreign>.
149.9. Þæt do on him dom awritynne wuldor þiss ys eallum halgum his <foreign>Vt faciant in eis iudicium conscriptum gloria hec est omnibus sanctis eius</foreign>.
150.1. Hergeað god on halgum his hegeaþ hine on trumnysse mægynys his <foreign>Lavdate devm in sanctis eius laudate eum in firmamento uirtutis eius</foreign>.
150.2. Hergeað hine on mihtum his hergeað hine æftyr mænigeo micylnysse his <foreign>Laudate eum in potentatibus eius laudate eum secundum multitudinem magnitudinis eius</foreign>.
150.3. Hergeað hine on swege byman hergeað hine on hearpan & citran vel hearpe <foreign>Laudate eum in sono tube laudate eum in psalterio et cythara</foreign>.
150.4. Hergeað hine on timpan vel o wifhearpan & þreate hergeað hine on strengum & organan <foreign>Laudate eum in tympano et choro laudate eum in chordis et organo</foreign>.
150.5. Hergeað hine on cimbalan wel hleoðriyndum hergeað hine on cimbalan wynsumnysse <foreign>Laudate eum in cymbalis bene sonantibus laudate eum in cymbalis iubilationis</foreign>.
150.6. Ælc gast herige drihtyn <foreign>omnis spiritus lavdet dominvm</foreign>.
